MODE)\n                return 'QUIT', {}\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN', {'sql': sql}\n    \n    def parse_alter_spec(self, table: str, alter_spec: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse ALTER TABLE specification.\n        \n        Handles:\n        - ADD COLUMN\n        - DROP COLUMN\n        - MODIFY COLUMN\n        - RENAME COLUMN\n        - ADD INDEX\n        - DROP INDEX\n        - ADD CONSTRAINT\n        - DROP CONSTRAINT\n        \"\"\"\n        alter_upper = alter_spec.upper().strip()\n        \n        # ADD COLUMN\n        add_col_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_col_match:\n            column_def = add_col_match.group(1)\n            col_info = self._parse_column_definition(column_def)\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': col_info\n            }\n        \n        # DROP COLUMN\n        drop_col_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)(?:\\s+(CASCADE))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_col_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': drop_col_match.group(1),\n                'cascade': drop_col_match.group(2) is not None\n            }\n        \n        # MODIFY COLUMN\n        modify_match = re.match(r'MODIFY\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)\\s+(\\w+)(?:\\s+(.+))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if modify_match:\n            return 'ALTER_MODIFY_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': modify_match.group(1),\n                'new_type': modify_match.group(2),\n                'constraints': modify_match.group(3) or ''\n            }\n        \n        # RENAME COLUMN\n        rename_match = re.match(r'RENAME\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)\\s+TO\\s+(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if rename_match:\n            return 'ALTER_RENAME_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'old_name': rename_match.group(1),\n                'new_name': rename_match.group(2)\n            }\n        \n        # ADD INDEX\n        add_idx_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\s+(?:\\w+\\s+)?\\(([^)]+)\\)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_idx_match:\n            columns = [c.strip() for c in add_idx_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_INDEX', {\n                'table': table,\n                'columns': columns\n            }\n        \n        # DROP INDEX\n        drop_idx_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\s+(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_idx_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_INDEX', {\n                'table': table,\n                'index_name': drop_idx_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        # ADD CONSTRAINT\n        add_cons_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\s+\\w+\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_cons_match:\n            constraint_def = add_cons_match.group(1)\n            # Parse the constraint\n            if constraint_def.upper().startswith('FOREIGN KEY'):\n                fk_match = re.match(\n                    r'FOREIGN\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s+REFERENCES\\s+(\\w+)\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)',\n                    constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE\n                )\n                if fk_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_FK', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                        'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                        'references_column': fk_match.group(3)\n                    }\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('UNIQUE'):\n                unique_match = re.match(r'UNIQUE\\s*\\(\\s*([^)]+)\\s*\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if unique_match:\n                    columns = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_UNIQUE', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'columns': columns\n                    }\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('CHECK'):\n                check_match = re.match(r'CHECK\\s*\\(([^)]+)\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if check_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_CHECK', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'expression': check_match.group(1)\n                    }\n        \n        # DROP CONSTRAINT\n        drop_cons_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\s+)?(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_cons_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_CONSTRAINT', {\n                'table': table,\n                'constraint_name': drop_cons_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN_ALTER', {'table': table, 'spec': alter_spec}\n            elif char == ')':\n                depth -= 1\n                current += char\n            elif char == ',' and depth == 0:\n                parts.append(current)\n                current = \"\"\n            else:\n                current += char\n        \n        if current.strip():\n            parts.append(current)\n        \n        return parts\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'GRANT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*GRANT\\s+(?P<privileges>[\\w\\s,]+)\\s+ON\\s+(?P<db>\\w+)\\.(?P<table>\\w+)\\s+TO\\s+(?P<username>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'REVOKE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*REVOKE\\s+(?P<privileges>[\\w\\s,]+)\\s+ON\\s+(?P<db>\\w+)\\.(?P<table>\\w+)\\s+FROM\\s+(?P<username>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'CREATE_ROLE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*CREATE\\s+ROLE\\s+(?P<role_name>\\w+)(?:\\s+DESCRIPTION\\s+(?P<description>\\'[^\\']*\\'|\\\"[^\\\"]*\\\"))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DROP_ROLE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DROP\\s+ROLE\\s+(?P<role_name>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'GRANT_ROLE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*GRANT\\s+ROLE\\s+(?P<role_name>\\w+)\\s+TO\\s+(?P<username>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'REVOKE_ROLE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*REVOKE\\s+ROLE\\s+(?P<role_name>\\w+)\\s+FROM\\s+(?P<username>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_GRANTS': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+GRANTS(?:\\s+FOR\\s+(?P<username>\\w+))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_ROLES': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+ROLES\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'AUDIT_LOG': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*AUDIT\\s+LOG(?:\\s+LIMIT\\s+(?P<limit>\\d+))?(?:\\s+USER\\s+(?P<user>\\w+))?(?:\\s+ACTION\\s+(?P<action>\\w+))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, sql: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse SQL-like command and return command type and parameters.\n        \n        Args:\n            sql: SQL command string\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (command_type, parameters_dict)\n    def _parse_column_definition(self, col_def: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse a single column definition.\"\"\"\n        col_info = {\n            'name': None,\n            'type': 'TEXT',\n            'primary_key': False,\n            'index': False,\n            'unique': False,\n            'foreign_key': None,\n            'check': None,\n            'nullable': True,\n            'default': None\n        }\n        \n        # Check for PRIMARY KEY constraint (can be inline or table-level)\n        pk_match = re.match(r'^\\s*PRIMARY\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if pk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'PRIMARY_KEY',\n                'column': pk_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        # Check for FOREIGN KEY table-level constraint\n        fk_match = re.match(\n            r'^\\s*FOREIGN\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s+REFERENCES\\s+(\\w+)\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)' +\n            r'(?:\\s+ON\\s+DELETE\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\s+ACTION))?' +\n            r'(?:\\s+ON\\s+UPDATE\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\s+ACTION))?\\s*$',\n            col_def, re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        if fk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'FOREIGN_KEY',\n                'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                'references_column': fk_match.group(3),\n                'on_delete': (fk_match.group(4) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_'),\n                'on_update': (fk_match.group(5) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_')\n            }\n        \n        # Check for UNIQUE constraint (table-level)\n        unique_match = re.match(r'^\\s*UNIQUE\\s*\\(\\s*([\\w\\s,]+)\\s*\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if unique_match:\n            cols = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'UNIQUE',\n                'columns': cols\n            }\n        \n        # Check for CHECK constraint\n        check_match = re.match(r'^\\s*CHECK\\s*\\((.+)\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if check_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'CHECK',\n                'expression': check_match.group(1).strip()\n            }\n        \n        # Parse regular column definition\n        # Pattern: name TYPE [constraints...]\n        # Handle REFERENCES inline: col TYPE REFERENCES table(col) [ON DELETE ...] [ON UPDATE ...]\n        parts = col_def.split()\n        if not parts:\n            return col_info\n        \n        col_info['name'] = parts[0]\n        \n        # Find type (second token if exists)\n        type_idx = 1\n        if len(parts) > 1 and not parts[1].upper() in ('PRIMARY', 'UNIQUE', 'REFERENCES', 'CHECK', 'NOT', 'DEFAULT'):\n            col_info['type'] = parts[1].upper()\n            type_idx = 2\n        \n        # Parse remaining constraints\n        i = type_idx\n        while i < len(parts):\n            token = parts[i].upper()\n            \n            if token == 'PRIMARY' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'KEY':\n                col_info['primary_key'] = True\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'INDEX':\n                col_info['index'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'UNIQUE':\n                col_info['unique'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'NOT' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'DEFAULT' and i + 1 < len(parts):\n                col_info['default'] = parts[i + 1]\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'REFERENCES':\n                # Parse REFERENCES clause\n                fk_info = self._parse_references_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['foreign_key'] = fk_info\n                i = fk_info.get('_end_index', i + 1)\n            elif token == 'CHECK':\n                # Parse CHECK clause\n                check_expr = self._parse_check_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['check'] = check_expr\n                i = check_expr.get('_end_index', i + 1) if isinstance(check_expr, dict) else i + 1\n            else:\n                i += 1\n        \n        return col_info\n        col_info = {\n            'name': None,\n            'type': 'TEXT',\n            'primary_key': False,\n            'index': False,\n            'unique': False,\n            'foreign_key': None,\n            'check': None,\n            'nullable': True,\n            'default': None\n        }\n        \n        # Check for PRIMARY KEY constraint (can be inline or table-level)\n        pk_match = re.match(r'^\\s*PRIMARY\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if pk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'PRIMARY_KEY',\n                'column': pk_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        # Check for FOREIGN KEY table-level constraint\n        fk_match = re.match(\n            r'^\\s*FOREIGN\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s+REFERENCES\\s+(\\w+)\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)' +\n            r'(?:\\s+ON\\s+DELETE\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\s+ACTION))?' +\n            r'(?:\\s+ON\\s+UPDATE\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\s+ACTION))?\\s*$',\n            col_def, re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        if fk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'FOREIGN_KEY',\n                'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                'references_column': fk_match.group(3),\n                'on_delete': (fk_match.group(4) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_'),\n                'on_update': (fk_match.group(5) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_')\n            }\n        \n        # Check for UNIQUE constraint (table-level)\n        unique_match = re.match(r'^\\s*UNIQUE\\s*\\(\\s*([\\w\\s,]+)\\s*\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if unique_match:\n            cols = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'UNIQUE',\n                'columns': cols\n            }\n        \n        # Check for CHECK constraint\n        check_match = re.match(r'^\\s*CHECK\\s*\\((.+)\\)\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if check_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'CHECK',\n                'expression': check_match.group(1).strip()\n            }\n        \n        # Parse regular column definition\n        # Pattern: name TYPE [constraints...]\n        # Handle REFERENCES inline: col TYPE REFERENCES table(col) [ON DELETE ...] [ON UPDATE ...]\n        parts = col_def.split()\n        if not parts:\n            return col_info\n        \n        col_info['name'] = parts[0]\n        \n        # Find type (second token if exists)\n        type_idx = 1\n        if len(parts) > 1 and not parts[1].upper() in ('PRIMARY', 'UNIQUE', 'REFERENCES', 'CHECK', 'NOT', 'DEFAULT'):\n            col_info['type'] = parts[1].upper()\n            type_idx = 2\n        \n        # Parse remaining constraints\n        i = type_idx\n        while i < len(parts):\n            token = parts[i].upper()\n            \n            if token == 'PRIMARY' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'KEY':\n                col_info['primary_key'] = True\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'INDEX':\n                col_info['index'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'UNIQUE':\n                col_info['unique'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'NOT' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'DEFAULT' and i + 1 < len(parts):\n                col_info['default'] = parts[i + 1]\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'REFERENCES':\n                # Parse REFERENCES clause\n                fk_info = self._parse_references_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['foreign_key'] = fk_info\n                i = fk_info.get('_end_index', i + 1)\n            elif token == 'CHECK':\n                # Parse CHECK clause\n                check_expr = self._parse_check_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['check'] = check_expr\n                i = check_expr.get('_end_index', i + 1) if isinstance(check_expr, dict) else i + 1\n            else:\n                i += 1\n        \n        return col_info\n    \n    def _parse_references_clause(self, parts: List[str], start_idx: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse REFERENCES table(column) [ON DELETE ...] [ON UPDATE ...].\"\"\"\n        fk_info = {\n            'references_table': None,\n            'references_column': None,\n            'on_delete': 'RESTRICT',\n            'on_update': 'RESTRICT'\n        }\n        \n        i = start_idx + 1\n        if i < len(parts):\n            # Get table name\n            ref_table = parts[i]\n            # Handle table(column) syntax\n            paren_match = re.match(r'(\\w+)\\((\\w+)\\)', ref_table)\n            if paren_match:\n                fk_info['references_table'] = paren_match.group(1)\n                fk_info['references_column'] = paren_match.group(2)\n                i += 1\n            elif i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].startswith('('):\n                fk_info['references_table'] = ref_table\n                col_match = re.match(r'\\((\\w+)\\)', parts[i + 1])\n                if col_match:\n                    fk_info['references_column'] = col_match.group(1)\n                i += 2\n        \n        # Parse ON DELETE and ON UPDATE\n        while i < len(parts):\n            token = parts[i].upper()\n            if token == 'ON' and i + 2 < len(parts):\n                action_type = parts[i + 1].upper()\n                action = parts[i + 2].upper()\n                if action_type == 'DELETE':\n                    fk_info['on_delete'] = action.replace(' ', '_')\n                    i += 3\n                elif action_type == 'UPDATE':\n                    fk_info['on_update'] = action.replace(' ', '_')\n                    i += 3\n                else:\n                    i += 1\n            else:\n                break\n        \n        fk_info['_end_index'] = i\n        return fk_info\n    \n    def _parse_check_clause(self, parts: List[str], start_idx: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse CHECK (expression).\"\"\"\n        # Join remaining parts and find the matching parenthesis\n        remaining = ' '.join(parts[start_idx + 1:])\n        paren_match = re.match(r'\\((.+)\\)', remaining)\n        if paren_match:\n            return {\n                'expression': paren_match.group(1).strip(),\n                '_end_index': len(parts)\n  re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_VIEWS': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+VIEWS\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'EXPLAIN': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*EXPLAIN\\s+(?P<target>.+)$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, sql: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse SQL-like command and return command type and parameters.\n        \n        Args:\n            sql: SQL command string\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (command_type, parameters_dict)\n        \"\"\"\n        sql = sql.strip()\n        \n        # Check for MATCH ... AGAINST first\n        match_against = self._parse_match_against(sql)\n        if match_against:\n            return match_against\n        \n        # Try each pattern\n        for cmd_type, pattern in self.patterns.items():\n            match = pattern.match(sql)\n            if match:\n                params = match.groupdict()\n                \n                # Handle ALTER specially\n                if cmd_type == 'ALTER':\n                    return self.parse_alter_spec(params['table'], params['alter_spec'])\n                \n                # Parse special fields\n                if 'columns' in params and params['columns']:\n                    if cmd_type in ('CREATE_FULLTEXT_INDEX',):\nn                        params['columns'] = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n                    else:\n                        params['columns'] = self._parse_select_columns(params['columns'])\n                \n                if 'values' in params and params['values']:\n                    params['values'] = self._parse_values(params['values'])\n                \n                if 'privileges' in params and params['privileges']:\n                    params['privileges'] = [p.strip().upper() for p in params['privileges'].split(',')]\n                \n                if 'description' in params and params['description']:\n                    params['description'] = params['description'].strip('\\'\"')\n                \n                if 'limit' in params and params['limit']:\n                    params['limit'] = int(params['limit'])\n                \n                return cmd_type, params\n        \n        # Check for simple commands\n        sql_upper = sql.upper()\n        if sql_upper == 'QUIT' or sql_upper == 'EXIT':\n            return 'QUIT', {}\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN', {'sql': sql}\n    \n    def parse_alter_spec(self, table: str, alter_spec: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse ALTER TABLE specification.\n        \n        Handles:\n        - ADD COLUMN\n        - DROP COLUMN\n        - MODIFY COLUMN\n        - RENAME COLUMN\n        - ADD INDEX\n        - DROP INDEX\n        - ADD CONSTRAINT\n        - DROP CONSTRAINT\n        \"\"\"\n        alter_upper = alter_spec.upper().strip()\n        \n        # ADD COLUMN\n        add_col_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_col_match:\n            column_def = add_col_match.group(1)\n            col_info = self._parse_column_definition(column_def)\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': col_info\n            }\n        \n        # DROP COLUMN\n        drop_col_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\\\w+)(?:\\\\s+(CASCADE))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_col_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': drop_col_match.group(1),\n                'cascade': drop_col_match.group(2) is not None\n            }\n        \n        # MODIFY COLUMN\n        modify_match = re.match(r'MODIFY\\\\s+(?:COLUMN\\\\s+)?(\\\\w+)\\\\s+(\\\\w+)(?:\\\\s+(.+))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if modify_match:\n            return 'ALTER_MODIFY_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': modify_match.group(1),\n                'new_type': modify_match.group(2),\n                'constraints': modify_match.group(3) or ''\n            }\n        \n        # RENAME COLUMN\n        rename_match = re.match(r'RENAME\\\\s+(?:COLUMN\\\\s+)?(\\\\w+)\\\\s+TO\\\\s+(\\\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if rename_match:\n            return 'ALTER_RENAME_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'old_name': rename_match.group(1),\n                'new_name': rename_match.group(2)\n            }\n        \n        # ADD INDEX\n        add_idx_match = re.match(r'ADD\\\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\\\s+(?:\\\\w+\\\\s+)?\\\\(([^)]+)\\\\)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_idx_match:\n            columns = [c.strip() for c in add_idx_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_INDEX', {\n                'table': table,\n                'columns': columns\n            }\n        \n        # DROP INDEX\n        drop_idx_match = re.match(r'DROP\\\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\\\s+(\\\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_idx_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_INDEX', {\n                'table': table,\n                'index_name': drop_idx_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        # ADD CONSTRAINT\n        add_cons_match = re.match(r'ADD\\\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\\\s+\\\\w+\\\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_cons_match:\n            constraint_def = add_cons_match.group(1)\n            # Parse the constraint\n            if constraint_def.upper().startswith('FOREIGN KEY'):\n                fk_match = re.match(\n                    r'FOREIGN\\\\s+KEY\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\)\\\\s+REFERENCES\\\\s+(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\)',\n                    constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE\n                )\n                if fk_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_FK', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                        'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                        'references_column': fk_match.group(3)\n                    }\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('UNIQUE'):\n                unique_match = re.match(r'UNIQUE\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*([^)]+)\\\\s*\\\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if unique_match:\n                    columns = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_UNIQUE', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'columns': columns\n                    }\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('CHECK'):\n                check_match = re.match(r'CHECK\\\\s*\\\\(([^)]+)\\\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if check_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_CHECK', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'expression': check_match.group(1)\n                    }\n        \n        # DROP CONSTRAINT\n        drop_cons_match = re.match(r'DROP\\\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\\\s+)?(\\\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_cons_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_CONSTRAINT', {\n                'table': table,\n                'constraint_name': drop_cons_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN_ALTER', {'table': table, 'spec': alter_spec}\n    \n    def _parse_match_against(self, sql: str) -> Optional[Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse MATCH ... AGAINST ... syntax for full-text search.\n        \n        Supports:\n        - MATCH (col1, col2) AGAINST ('search term')\n        - MATCH (col1, col2) AGAINST ('search term' IN NATURAL LANGUAGE MODE)\n        - MATCH (col1, col2) AGAINST ('search term' IN BOOLEAN MODE)\n        - MATCH (col1, col2) AGAINST ('search term' WITH QUERY EXPANSION)\n        \"\"\"\n        pattern = re.compile(\n            r'^\\\\s*MATCH\\\\s*\\\\((?P<columns>[\\\\w\\\\s,]+)\\\\)\\\\s+AGAINST\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*[\\\\'\\\\\"](?P<query>[^\\\\'\\\"]+)[\\\\'\\\"]\\\\s*(?:\\\\s+IN\\\\s+(?P<mode>[\\\\w\\\\s]+)\\\\s+MODE)?(?:\\\\s+(?P<expansion>WITH\\\\s+QUERY\\\\s+EXPANSION))?\\\\s*\\\\)\\\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        \n        match = pattern.match(sql)\n        if match:\n            params = match.groupdict()\n            columns = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n            \n            # Determine search mode\n            mode = 'NATURAL'\n            if params.get('mode'):\n                mode_str = params['mode'].upper()\n                if 'BOOLEAN' in mode_str:\n                    mode = 'BOOLEAN'\n                elif 'NATURAL' in mode_str:\n                    mode = 'NATURAL'\n            \n            # Check for query expansion\n            if params.get('expansion'):\n                mode = 'EXPANSION'\n            \n            return 'MATCH_AGAINST', {\n                'columns': columns,\n                'query': params['query'],\n                'mode': mode\n            }\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def _parse_select_columns(self, columns_str: str) -> List[Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse SELECT column list with JSON extraction support.\"\"\"\n        columns = []\n        parts = self._split_columns(columns_str)\n        \n        for part in parts:\n            part = part.strip()\n            if not part:\n                continue\n            \n            # Check for JSON extraction: column->path or column->>path\n            json_match = re.match(r'(\\\\w+)(->>?)(.+)', part)\n            if json_match:\n                col_name = json_match.group(1)\n                operator = json_match.group(2)\n                json_path = json_match.group(3).strip()\n                \n                columns.append({\n                    'name': col_name,\n                    'json_path': json_path,\n                    'json_as_text': operator == '->>'\n                })\n            # Check for aliased column: column AS alias\n            elif ' AS ' in part.upper():\n                parts = part.split()\n                col_name = parts[0]\n                alias = parts[-1]\n                columns.append({\n                    'name': col_name,\n                    'alias': alias\n                })\n            else:\n                columns.append(part)\n        \n        return columns\n    \n    def _split_columns(self, args_str: str) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"Split comma-separated columns respecting parentheses.\"\"\"\n        parts = []\n        current = \"\"\n        depth = 0\n        \n        for char in args_str:\n            if char == '(':\n                depth += 1\n                current += char\n            elif char == ')':\n                depth -= 1\n                current += char\n            elif char == ',' and depth == 0:\n                parts.append(current)\n                current = \"\"\n            else:\n                current += char\n        \n        if current.strip():\n            parts.append(current)\n        \n        return parts\n    \n    def _parse_column_definition(self, col_def: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse a single column definition.\"\"\"\n        col_info = {\n            'name': None,\n            'type': 'TEXT',\n            'primary_key': False,\n            'index': False,\n            'unique': False,\n            'foreign_key': None,\n            'check': None,\n            'nullable': True,\n            'default': None\n        }\n        \n        # Check for PRIMARY KEY constraint (can be inline or table-level)\n        pk_match = re.match(r'^\\\\s*PRIMARY\\\\s+KEY\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\)\\\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if pk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'PRIMARY_KEY',\n                'column': pk_match.group(1)\n            }\n        \n        # Check for FOREIGN KEY table-level constraint\n        fk_match = re.match(\n            r'^\\\\s*FOREIGN\\\\s+KEY\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\)\\\\s+REFERENCES\\\\s+(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*(\\\\w+)\\\\s*\\\\)' +\n            r'(?:\\\\s+ON\\\\s+DELETE\\\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\\\s+ACTION))?' +\n            r'(?:\\\\s+ON\\\\s+UPDATE\\\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\\\s+ACTION))?\\\\s*$',\n            col_def, re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        if fk_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'FOREIGN_KEY',\n                'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                'references_column': fk_match.group(3),\n                'on_delete': (fk_match.group(4) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_'),\n                'on_update': (fk_match.group(5) or 'RESTRICT').upper().replace(' ', '_')\n            }\n        \n        # Check for UNIQUE constraint (table-level)\n        unique_match = re.match(r'^\\\\s*UNIQUE\\\\s*\\\\(\\\\s*([\\\\w\\\\s,]+)\\\\s*\\\\)\\\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if unique_match:\n            cols = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'UNIQUE',\n                'columns': cols\n            }\n        \n        # Check for CHECK constraint\n        check_match = re.match(r'^\\\\s*CHECK\\\\s*\\\\((.+)\\\\)\\\\s*$', col_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if check_match:\n            return {\n                'constraint_type': 'CHECK',\n                'expression': check_match.group(1).strip()\n            }\n        \n        # Parse regular column definition\n        # Pattern: name TYPE [constraints...]\n        # Handle REFERENCES inline: col TYPE REFERENCES table(col) [ON DELETE ...] [ON UPDATE ...]\n        parts = col_def.split()\n        if not parts:\n            return col_info\n        \n        col_info['name'] = parts[0]\n        \n        # Find type (second token if exists)\n        type_idx = 1\n        if len(parts) > 1 and not parts[1].upper() in ('PRIMARY', 'UNIQUE', 'REFERENCES', 'CHECK', 'NOT', 'DEFAULT'):\n            col_info['type'] = parts[1].upper()\n            type_idx = 2\n        \n        # Parse remaining constraints\n        i = type_idx\n        while i < len(parts):\n            token = parts[i].upper()\n            \n            if token == 'PRIMARY' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'KEY':\n                col_info['primary_key'] = True\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'INDEX':\n                col_info['index'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'UNIQUE':\n                col_info['unique'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'NOT' and i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].upper() == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = False\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'NULL':\n                col_info['nullable'] = True\n                i += 1\n            elif token == 'DEFAULT' and i + 1 < len(parts):\n                col_info['default'] = parts[i + 1]\n                i += 2\n            elif token == 'REFERENCES':\n                # Parse REFERENCES clause\n                fk_info = self._parse_references_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['foreign_key'] = fk_info\n                i = fk_info.get('_end_index', i + 1)\n            elif token == 'CHECK':\n                # Parse CHECK clause\n                check_expr = self._parse_check_clause(parts, i)\n                col_info['check'] = check_expr\n                i = check_expr.get('_end_index', i + 1) if isinstance(check_expr, dict) else i + 1\n            else:\n                i += 1\n        \n        return col_info\n    \n    def _parse_references_clause(self, parts: List[str], start_idx: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse REFERENCES table(column) [ON DELETE ...] [ON UPDATE ...].\"\"\"\n        fk_info = {\n            'references_table': None,\n            'references_column': None,\n            'on_delete': 'RESTRICT',\n            'on_update': 'RESTRICT'\n        }\n        \n        i = start_idx + 1\n        if i < len(parts):\n            # Get table name\n            ref_table = parts[i]\n            # Handle table(column) syntax\n            paren_match = re.match(r'(\\\\w+)\\\\((\\\\w+)\\\\)', ref_table)\n            if paren_match:\n                fk_info['references_table'] = paren_match.group(1)\n                fk_info['references_column'] = paren_match.group(2)\n                i += 1\n            elif i + 1 < len(parts) and parts[i + 1].startswith('('):\n                fk_info['references_table'] = ref_table\n                col_match = re.match(r'\\\\((\\\\w+)\\\\)', parts[i + 1])\n                if col_match:\n                    fk_info['references_column'] = col_match.group(1)\n                i += 2\n        \n        # Parse ON DELETE and ON UPDATE\n        while i < len(parts):\n            token = parts[i].upper()\n            if token == 'ON' and i + 2 < len(parts):\n                action_type = parts[i + 1].upper()\n                action = parts[i + 2].upper()\n                if action_type == 'DELETE':\n                    fk_info['on_delete'] = action.replace(' ', '_')\n                    i += 3\n                elif action_type == 'UPDATE':\n                    fk_info['on_update'] = action.replace(' ', '_')\n                    i += 3\n                else:\n                    i += 1\n            else:\n                break\n        \n        fk_info['_end_index'] = i\n        return fk_info\n    \n    def _parse_check_clause(self, parts: List[str], start_idx: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse CHECK (expression).\"\"\"\n        # Join remaining parts and find the matching parenthesis\n        remaining = ' '.join(parts[start_idx + 1:])\n        paren_match = re.match(r'\\\\((.+)\\\\)', remaining)\n        if paren_match:\n            return {\n                'expression': paren_match.group(1).strip(),\n                '_end_index': len(parts)\n            }\n        return {'expression': remaining.strip(), '_end_index': len(parts)}\n    \n    def _parse_values(self, values_str: str) -> List[Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse VALUES clause.\"\"\"\n        values = []\n        for val in values_str.split(','):\n            val = val.strip()\n            # Try to convert to number\n            try:\n                if '.' in val:\n                    values.append(float(val))\n                else:\n                    values.append(int(val))\n            except ValueError:\n                # Remove quotes if present\n                if (val.startswith(\"'\") and val.endswith(\"'\")) or \\\n                   (val.startswith('\"') and val.endswith('\"')):\n                    val = val[1:-1]\n                values.append(val)\n        return values\n\n\nclass BackupRestoreParser:\n    \"\"\"Parser for backup and restore commands with encryption and compression support.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.patterns = {\n            'BACKUP': re.compile(\n                r'^\\\\s*BACKUP\\\\s+(?:DATABASE\\\\s+)?(?P<db_name>\\\\w+)' +\n                r'(?:\\\\s+TO\\\\s+(?P<backup_path>\\\\S+))?' +\n                r'(?:\\\\s+WITH\\\\s+(?P<options>.+))?\\\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'RESTORE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\\\s*RESTORE\\\\s+(?:DATABASE\\\\s+)?(?P<db_name>\\\\w+)' +\n                r'(?:\\\\s+FROM\\\\s+(?P<backup_path>\\\\S+))?' +\n                r'(?:\\\\s+WITH\\\\s+(?P<options>.+))?\\\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, sql: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Parse backup/restore commands.\"\"\"\n        sql = sql.strip()\n        \n        for cmd_type, pattern in self.patterns.items():\n            match = pattern.match(sql)\n            if match:\n                params = match.groupdict()\n                \n                # Parse options (ENCRYPTION, COMPRESSION, etc.)\n                options_str = params.get('options', '')\n                if options_str:\n                    options = self._parse_options(options_str)\n                    params.update(options)\n                \n                return cmd_type, params\n        \n        # Fall back to regular parser\n        regular_parser = CommandParser()\n        return regular_parser.parse(sql)\n    \n    def _parse_options(self, options_str: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse WITH options for backup/restore.\"\"\"\n        options = {}\n        \n        # ENCRYPTION 'password'\n        enc_match = re.search(r\"ENCRYPTION\\\\s+['\\\\\\\"]([^'\\\\\\\"]+)['\\\\\\\"]\", options_str, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if enc_match:\n            options['encryption'] = enc_match.group(1)\n        \n        # COMPRESSION 'gzip|lz4|zstd|none'\n        comp_match = re.search(r\"COMPRESSION\\\\s+(\\\\w+)\", options_str, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if comp_match:\n            options['compression'] = comp_match.group(1).lower()\n        \n        # LEVEL 1-9\n        level_match = re.search(r\"LEVEL\\\\s+(\\\\d+)\", options_str, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if level_match:\n            options['compression_level'] = int(level_match.group(1))\n        \n        return options\n\n\n# Example usage\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    parser = CommandParser()\n    \n    test_commands = [\n        \"CREATE DATABASE testdb\",\n        \"USE testdb\",\n        \"CREATE TABLE users (id INT, name TEXT)\",\n        \"INSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice')\",\n        \"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = 1\",\n        \"UPDATE users SET name = 'Bob' WHERE id = 1\",\n        \"DELETE FROM users WHERE id = 1\",\n        \"DROP TABLE users\",\n        \"DROP DATABASE testdb\",\n        \"GRANT SELECT, INSERT ON testdb.users TO alice\",\n        \"REVOKE DELETE ON testdb.users FROM alice\",\n        \"CREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only access'\",\n        \"GRANT ROLE readonly TO alice\",\n        \"SHOW GRANTS FOR alice\",\n        \"SHOW ROLES\",\n        # re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DROP_FULLTEXT_INDEX': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DROP\\s+FULLTEXT\\s+INDEX\\s+(?P<index_name>\\w+)?\\s*ON\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_VIEWS': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+VIEWS\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'EXPLAIN': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*EXPLAIN\\s+(?P<target>.+)$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, sql: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse SQL-like command and return command type and parameters.\n        \"\"\"\n        sql = sql.strip()\n        \n        # Check for MATCH ... AGAINST first\n        match_against = self._parse_match_against(sql)\n        if match_against:\n            return match_against\n        \n        # Try each pattern\n        for cmd_type, pattern in self.patterns.items():\n            match = pattern.match(sql)\n            if match:\n                params = match.groupdict()\n                \n                # Handle ALTER specially\n                if cmd_type == 'ALTER':\n                    return self.parse_alter_spec(params['table'], params['alter_spec'])\n                \n                # Parse special fields\n                if 'columns' in params and params['columns']:\n                    if cmd_type == 'CREATE_FULLTEXT_INDEX':\n                        params['columns'] = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n                    else:\n                        params['columns'] = self._parse_select_columns(params['columns'])\n                \n                if 'values' in params and params['values']:\n                    params['values'] = self._parse_values(params['values'])\n                \n                if 'privileges' in params and params['privileges']:\n                    params['privileges'] = [p.strip().upper() for p in params['privileges'].split(',')]\n                \n                if 'description' in params and params['description']:\n                    params['description'] = params['description'].strip('\\'\"')\n                \n                if 'limit' in params and params['limit']:\n                    params['limit'] = int(params['limit'])\n                \n                return cmd_type, params\n        \n        # Check for simple commands\n        sql_upper = sql.upper()\n        if sql_upper == 'QUIT' or sql_upper == 'EXIT':\n            return 'QUIT', {}\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN', {'sql': sql}\n    \n    def parse_alter_spec(self, table: str, alter_spec: str) -> Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Parse ALTER TABLE specification.\"\"\"\n        alter_upper = alter_spec.upper().strip()\n        \n        # ADD COLUMN\n        add_col_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_col_match:\n            column_def = add_col_match.group(1)\n            col_info = self._parse_column_definition(column_def)\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_COLUMN', {'table': table, 'column': col_info}\n        \n        # DROP COLUMN\n        drop_col_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)(?:\\s+(CASCADE))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_col_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': drop_col_match.group(1),\n                'cascade': drop_col_match.group(2) is not None\n            }\n        \n        # MODIFY COLUMN\n        modify_match = re.match(r'MODIFY\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)\\s+(\\w+)(?:\\s+(.+))?', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if modify_match:\n            return 'ALTER_MODIFY_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'column': modify_match.group(1),\n                'new_type': modify_match.group(2),\n                'constraints': modify_match.group(3) or ''\n            }\n        \n        # RENAME COLUMN\n        rename_match = re.match(r'RENAME\\s+(?:COLUMN\\s+)?(\\w+)\\s+TO\\s+(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if rename_match:\n            return 'ALTER_RENAME_COLUMN', {\n                'table': table,\n                'old_name': rename_match.group(1),\n                'new_name': rename_match.group(2)\n            }\n        \n        # ADD INDEX\n        add_idx_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\s+(?:\\w+\\s+)?\\(([^)]+)\\)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_idx_match:\n            columns = [c.strip() for c in add_idx_match.group(1).split(',')]\n            return 'ALTER_ADD_INDEX', {'table': table, 'columns': columns}\n        \n        # DROP INDEX\n        drop_idx_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:INDEX|KEY)\\s+(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_idx_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_INDEX', {'table': table, 'index_name': drop_idx_match.group(1)}\n        \n        # ADD CONSTRAINT\n        add_cons_match = re.match(r'ADD\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\s+\\w+\\s+)?(.+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if add_cons_match:\n            constraint_def = add_cons_match.group(1)\n            if constraint_def.upper().startswith('FOREIGN KEY'):\n                fk_match = re.match(\n                    r'FOREIGN\\s+KEY\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)\\s+REFERENCES\\s+(\\w+)\\s*\\(\\s*(\\w+)\\s*\\)',\n                    constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE\n                )\n                if fk_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_FK', {\n                        'table': table,\n                        'column': fk_match.group(1),\n                        'references_table': fk_match.group(2),\n                        'references_column': fk_match.group(3)\n                    }\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('UNIQUE'):\n                unique_match = re.match(r'UNIQUE\\s*\\(\\s*([^)]+)\\s*\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if unique_match:\n                    columns = [c.strip() for c in unique_match.group(1).split(',')]\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_UNIQUE', {'table': table, 'columns': columns}\n            elif constraint_def.upper().startswith('CHECK'):\n                check_match = re.match(r'CHECK\\s*\\(([^)]+)\\)', constraint_def, re.IGNORECASE)\n                if check_match:\n                    return 'ALTER_ADD_CHECK', {'table': table, 'expression': check_match.group(1)}\n        \n        # DROP CONSTRAINT\n        drop_cons_match = re.match(r'DROP\\s+(?:CONSTRAINT\\s+)?(\\w+)', alter_spec, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if drop_cons_match:\n            return 'ALTER_DROP_CONSTRAINT', {'table': table, 'constraint_name': drop_cons_match.group(1)}\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN_ALTER', {'table': table, 'spec': alter_spec}\n    \n    def _parse_match_against(self, sql: str) -> Optional[Tuple[str, Dict[str, Any]]]:\n        \"\"\"Parse MATCH ... AGAINST ... syntax for full-text search.\"\"\"\n        pattern = re.compile(\n            r'^\\s*MATCH\\s*\\((?P<columns>[\\w\\s,]+)\\)\\s+AGAINST\\s*\\(\\s*[\\'\\\"](?P<query>[^\\'\\\"]+)[\\'\\\"]\\s*(?:\\s+IN\\s+(?P<mode>[\\w\\s]+)\\s+MODE)?(?:\\s+(?P<expansion>WITH\\s+QUERY\\s+EXPANSION))?\\s*\\)\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        \n        match = pattern.match(sql)\n        if match:\n            params = match.groupdict()\n            columns = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n            \n            mode = 'NATURAL'\n            if params.get('mode'):\n                mode_str = params['mode'].upper()\n                if 'BOOLEAN' in mode_str:\n                    mode = 'BOOLEAN'\n                elif 'NATURAL' in mode_str:\n                    mode = 'NATURAL'\n            \n            if params.get('expansion'):\n _parse_select_columns(self, columns_str: str) -> List[Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse SELECT column list with JSON extraction support.\"\"\"\n        columns = []\n        parts = self._split_columns(columns_str)\n        \n        for part in parts:\n            part = part.strip()\n            if not part:\n                continue\n            \n            # Check for JSON extraction: column->path or column->>path\n            json_match = re.match(r'(\\w+)(->>?)(.+)', part)\n            if json_match:\n                col_name = json_match.group(1)\n                operator = json_match.group(2)\n                json_path = json_match.group(3).strip()\n                columns.append({\n                    'name': col_name,\n                    'json_path': json_path,\n                    'json_as_text': operator == '->>'\n                })\n            elif ' AS ' in part.upper():\n                parts = part.split()\n                col_name = parts[0]\n                alias = parts[-1]\n                columns.append({'name': col_name, 'alias': alias})\n            else:\n                columns.append(part)\n        \n        return columns\n    \n    def _split_columns(self, args_str: str) -> List[str]:\n        \"\"\"Split comma-separated columns respecting parentheses.\"\"\"\n        parts = []\n        current = \"\"\n        depth = 0\n        \n        for char in args_str:\n            if char == '(':\n                depth += 1\n                current += char\n            elif char == ')':\n                depth -= 1\n                current += char\n            elif char == ',' and depth == 0:\n                parts.append(current)\n                current = \"\"\n            else:\n                current += char\n        \n        if current.strip():\n            parts.append(current)\n        \n        return parts\n    \n    def _parse_column_definition(self, col_def: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse a single column definition.\"\"\"\n        col_info = {\n            'name': None,\n            'type': 'TEXT',\n            'primary_key': False,\n            'index': False,\n r'(?:\\s+ON\\s+UPDATE\\s+(CASCADE|SET\\s+NULL|RESTRICT|NO\\s+ACTION))?\\s*$',\n            col_def, re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        if fk_match:\n            return {\n <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "Now let me add subquery parsing methods to the parser:  <ReplaceLine>\n<fileName>parser.py</fileName>\n<fromLine>170</fromLine>\n<toLine>200</toLine>\n<replacement>        return 'UNKNOWN', {'sql': sql}\n    \n    def _parse_where_clause(self, where_str: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse WHERE clause with support for subqueries.\n        \n        Supports:\n        - Simple conditions: col = value\n        - IN/NOT IN subqueries: col IN (SELECT ...)\n        - EXISTS/NOT EXISTS: EXISTS (SELECT ...)\n        - Scalar subqueries: col = (SELECT ...)\n        \"\"\"\n        where_str = where_str.strip()\n        conditions = []\n        \n        # Remove outer parentheses if present\n        while subquery_str.startswith('(') and subquery_str.endswith(')'):\n            inner = subquery_str[1:-1].strip()\n            # Check if parentheses are balanced\n            depth = 0\n            valid = True\n            for char in inner:\n                if char == '(':\n                    depth += 1\n                elif char == ')':\n                    depth -= 1\n                    if depth < 0:\n                        valid = False\n                        break\n            if valid and depth == 0:\n                subquery_str = inner\n            else:\n                break\n        \n        # Simple heuristic: check for table.column references\n        # that don't match the subquery's FROM table\n        outer_refs = re.findall(r'(\\\\w+)\\\\.(\\\\w+)', subquery_str)\n        \n        # Get subquery's table\n        from_match = re.search(r'FROM\\\\s+(\\\\w+)', subquery_str, re.IGNORECASE)\n        if not from_match:\n            return False\n        \n        subquery_table = from_match.group(1)\n        \n        # Check cache\n        cache_key = self._get_cache_key(query)\n        if use_cache:\n            cached_plan = self.plan_cache.get(cache_key)\n            if cached_plan:\n                return cached_plan\n        \n        # <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# KosDB v3.1.0\n\nA high-performance, feature-rich LevelDB-based database server with SQL-like interface, replication, TLS encryption, GPU acceleration, and comprehensive audit logging.\n\n## Features\n\n### Core Database\n- **SQL-like Interface**: Familiar CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE commands\n- **Multiple Databases**: Support for multiple named databases\n- **Table Schema**: Define columns with types (INT, TEXT, FLOAT, etc.)\n- **Transactions**: ACID-compliant operations\n- **Indexing**: Primary and secondary index support\n\n### Security (New in v3.1.0)\n- **TLS/SSL Encryption**: Secure client-server communication\n  - Certificate-based authentication\n  - Self-signed certificate generation\n  - Client certificate verification (mTLS)\n- **At-Rest Encryption**: AES-256-GCM database encryption\n  - PBKDF2 key derivation\n  - Master key rotation support\n- **Audit Logging**: Comprehensive operation logging\n  - Multiple output targets (file, syslog, webhook)\n  - Log rotation and compression\n  - Sensitive command masking\n\n### Authentication & Authorization\n- **Database-backed Authentication**: Username/password with bcrypt hashing\n- **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)**: Create roles and assign to users\n- **Granular Permissions**: SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, DROP, ALTER, INDEX, ADMIN\n- **Column-level Security**: Restrict access to specific columns\n- **Session Management**: JWT-based sessions with TTL\n\n### Replication & High Availability\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Automatic failover support\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multi-master with conflict resolution\n- **Async Replication**: Non-blocking replication\n- **Replication Lag Monitoring**: Track replication health\n\n### Performance Features\n- **GPU Acceleration**: CUDA-powered query processing\n  - Vector operations\n  - Matrix multiplication\n  - Sorting algorithms\n- **Connection Pooling**: Efficient connection management\n- **Query Caching**: Result cache for frequent queries\n- **Compression**: Multiple algorithms (gzip, lz4, zstd)\n\n### Backup & Recovery\n- **Hot Backups**: Non-blocking backup operations\n- **Encrypted Backups**: Password-protected backup files\n- **Compression Options**: gzip, lz4, zstd\n- **Point-in-Time Recovery**: Restore to specific timestamp\n- **Integrity Verification**: SHA-256 checksums\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Installation\n\n```bash\n# Clone repository\ngit clone https://github.com/yourusername/kosdb.git\ncd kosdb\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Optional: Install GPU support\npip install pycuda  # For CUDA acceleration\n\n# Optional: Install encryption\npip install cryptography  # For TLS and at-rest encryption\n```\n\n### Basic Usage\n\n```bash\n# Start server with default config\npython server.py\n\n# Or specify configuration file\npython server.py -c config.json\n\n# Create admin user\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin --prepare_password secret123\n```\n\n### Client Connection\n\n```bash\n# Connect with CLI client\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 -u admin -P secret123\n\n# Or use with TLS\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Basic Configuration (config.json)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.1.0\",\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9999,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\"\n  },\n  \"database\": {\n    \"engine\": \"leveldb\",\n    \"compression\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### TLS Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Audit Logging Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"audit_logging\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"log_dir\": \"./audit_logs\",\n    \"max_size_mb\": 100,\n    \"max_age_days\": 30,\n    \"targets\": [\"file\", \"syslog\"],\n    \"exclude_commands\": [\"PING\"],\n    \"mask_commands\": [\"PASS\", \"PASSWORD\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### GPU Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8,\n    \"kernels\": [\"vector_ops\", \"matrix_mult\", \"sort\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\nSee [Configuration Guide](README_CONFIG.md) for complete documentation.\n\n## SQL Commands\n\n### Database Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create database\nCREATE DATABASE mydb;\n\n-- Use database\nUSE mydb;\n\n-- Drop database\nDROP DATABASE mydb;\n```\n\n### Table Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create table\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT,\n    email TEXT,\n    age INT\n);\n\n-- Describe table\nDESCRIBE users;\n\n-- Drop table\nDROP TABLE users;\n```\n\n### Data Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Insert\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 30);\n\n-- Select\nSELECT * FROM users;\nSELECT name, email FROM users WHERE age > 25;\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE name LIKE 'A%';\n\n-- Update\nUPDATE users SET age = 31 WHERE id = 1;\n\n-- Delete\nDELETE FROM users WHERE id = 1;\n```\n\n### User Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create user\nCREATE USER alice PASSWORD 'secret123';\n\n-- Grant privileges\nGRANT SELECT, INSERT ON mydb.users TO alice;\n\n-- Revoke privileges\nREVOKE DELETE ON mydb.users FROM alice;\n\n-- Show grants\nSHOW GRANTS FOR alice;\n```\n\n### Role Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create role\nCREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only access';\n\n-- Grant privileges to role\nGRANT SELECT ON *.* TO readonly;\n\n-- Assign role to user\nGRANT ROLE readonly TO alice;\n\n-- Show roles\nSHOW ROLES;\n```\n\n### Backup Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Backup with encryption\nBACKUP DATABASE mydb TO /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword' COMPRESSION gzip;\n\n-- Restore with encryption\nRESTORE DATABASE mydb FROM /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword';\n```\n\n## Environment Variables\n\nSensitive configuration values can be stored in environment variables:\n\n```bash\n# Encryption passphrase\nexport KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE=\"my-secret-key\"\n\n# TLS certificate password\nexport KOSDB_TLS_PASSWORD=\"cert-password\"\n\n# Backup encryption\nexport KOSDB_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE=\"backup-secret\"\n\n# JWT secret\nexport KOSDB_JWT_SECRET=\"jwt-signing-key\"\n```\n\nReference in config.json:\n```json\n{\n  \"database\": {\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Security Hardening\n\n### TLS Setup\n\n1. Generate CA and server certificates:\n```bash\n# Generate CA\nopenssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout ca.key -out ca.crt -days 365 -nodes\n\n# Generate server certificate\nopenssl req -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout server.key -out server.csr -nodes\nopenssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 365\n```\n\n2. Configure server:\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n3. Connect client with TLS:\n```bash\npython cli.py --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n### Encryption Best Practices\n\n1. **Use strong passphrases** (minimum 16 characters)\n2. **Store keys securely** (use key files with restricted permissions)\n3. **Rotate keys regularly** (use `ROTATE KEY` command)\n4. **Backup keys separately** from encrypted data\n5. **Enable audit logging** for encryption operations\n\n## Performance Tuning\n\n### GPU Acceleration\n\nEnable GPU for large-scale operations:\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8\n  }\n}\n```\n\nGPU-accelerated operations:\n- Vector mathematical operations\n- Matrix multiplication\n- Large dataset sorting\n- Aggregate functions\n\n### Connection Pooling\n\n```json\n{\n  \"performance\": {\n    \"connection_pool_min\": 5,\n    \"connection_pool_max\": 20,\n    \"query_cache_size\": 1000\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Health Check\n\n```bash\n# Check server health\npython cli.py -c \"SHOW STATUS\"\n```\n\n### Metrics\n\nEnable Prometheus metrics:\n```json\n{\n  \"monitoring\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"metrics_port\": 9090,\n    \"prometheus_enabled\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\nAccess metrics at `http://localhost:9090/metrics`\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Issues\n\n- Verify server is running: `python cli.py -c \"PING\"`\n- Check firewall rules for port 9999\n- Verify TLS certificates are valid\n\n### Performance Issues\n\n- Check query cache hit rate\n- Monitor replication lag\n- Review slow query log\n\n### Encryption Issues\n\n- Verify passphrase is correct\n- Check key file permissions (should be 600)\n- Ensure cryptography library is installed\n\n## API Reference\n\nSee [API Documentation](docs/API.md) for detailed command reference.\n\n## Contributing\n\nSee [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md) for contribution guidelines.\n\n## License\n\nMIT License - see [LICENSE](LICENSE) for details.\n\n## Changelog\n\nSee [CHANGELOG.md](CHANGELOG.md) for version history.\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 41, "timestamp": 1783744160.74144, "date": "2026-07-11", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>README.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># KosDB v3.2.0\n\nA high-performance, feature-rich LevelDB-based database server with SQL-like interface, replication, TLS encryption, GPU acceleration, comprehensive audit logging, and advanced query capabilities.\n\n## Features\n\n### Core Database\n- **SQL-like Interface**: Familiar CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE commands\n- **Multiple Databases**: Support for multiple named databases\n- **Table Schema**: Define columns with types (INT, TEXT, FLOAT, JSON, etc.)\n- **Transactions**: ACID-compliant operations with BEGIN, COMMIT, ROLLBACK\n- **Indexing**: Primary, secondary, and full-text index support\n- **Views**: Virtual tables based on SELECT queries\n- **Subqueries**: Scalar, IN/NOT IN, EXISTS/NOT EXISTS, correlated subqueries\n\n### Security (New in v3.1.0+)\n- **TLS/SSL Encryption**: Secure client-server communication\n  - Certificate-based authentication\n  - Self-signed certificate generation\n  - Client certificate verification (mTLS)\n- **At-Rest Encryption**: AES-256-GCM database encryption\n  - PBKDF2 key derivation\n  - Master key rotation support\n- **Audit Logging**: Comprehensive operation logging\n  - Multiple output targets (file, syslog, webhook)\n  - Log rotation and compression\n  - Sensitive command masking\n\n### Authentication & Authorization\n- **Database-backed Authentication**: Username/password with bcrypt hashing\n- **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)**: Create roles and assign to users\n- **Granular Permissions**: SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, DROP, ALTER, INDEX, REFERENCES, ADMIN\n- **Column-level Security**: Restrict access to specific columns\n- **Session Management**: JWT-based sessions with TTL\n\n### Replication & High Availability\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Automatic failover support\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multi-master with conflict resolution\n- **Async Replication**: Non-blocking replication\n- **Replication Lag Monitoring**: Track replication health\n\n### Query Optimization (New in v3.2.0)\n- **Query Plan Caching**: LRU cache for parsed execution plans\n- **Cost-Based Optimizer**: Statistics-driven plan selection\n- **Semi-Join Optimization**: Efficient IN/EXISTS subquery execution\n- **Index Advisor**: Automatic index recommendations\n- **Query Statistics**: Execution metrics and profiling\n\n### Advanced SQL (New in v3.2.0)\n- **CHECK Constraints**: Data validation with complex expressions\n- **Foreign Keys**: Referential integrity with CASCADE/SET NULL/RESTRICT\n- **ALTER TABLE**: Add/drop/modify columns, indexes, constraints\n- **JSON Support**: Native JSON columns with path extraction\n- **Full-Text Search**: MATCH ... AGAINST syntax with relevance scoring\n- **Subqueries**: Scalar, IN, EXISTS, correlated subqueries\n\n### Performance Features\n- **GPU Acceleration**: CUDA-powered query processing\n  - Vector operations\n  - Matrix multiplication\n  - Sorting algorithms\n- **Connection Pooling**: Efficient connection management\n- **Query Caching**: Result cache for frequent queries\n- **Plan Caching**: Execution plan cache for repeated queries\n- **Compression**: Multiple algorithms (gzip, lz4, zstd)\n\n### Monitoring (New in v3.2.0)\n- **Prometheus Metrics**: Query counts, latency, cache hit rates\n- **Health Checks**: Liveness and readiness endpoints\n- **Detailed Status**: Server status via HTTP API\n- **Cache Statistics**: Plan cache performance metrics\n\n### Backup & Recovery\n- **Hot Backups**: Non-blocking backup operations\n- **Encrypted Backups**: Password-protected backup files\n- **Compression Options**: gzip, lz4, zstd\n- **Point-in-Time Recovery**: Restore to specific timestamp\n- **Integrity Verification**: SHA-256 checksums\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Installation\n\n```bash\n# Clone repository\ngit clone https://github.com/yourusername/kosdb.git\ncd kosdb\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Optional: Install GPU support\npip install pycuda  # For CUDA acceleration\n\n# Optional: Install encryption\npip install cryptography  # For TLS and at-rest encryption\n```\n\n### Basic Usage\n\n```bash\n# Start server with default config\npython server.py\n\n# Or specify configuration file\npython server.py -c config.json\n\n# Create admin user\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin --prepare_password secret123\n```\n\n### Client Connection\n\n```bash\n# Connect with CLI client\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 -u admin -P secret123\n\n# Or use with TLS\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Basic Configuration (config.json)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9999,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\"\n  },\n  \"database\": {\n    \"engine\": \"leveldb\",\n    \"compression\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### TLS Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Metrics and Monitoring (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15,\n    \"retention_days\": 30\n  }\n}\n```\n\nAccess metrics at:\n- `http://localhost:9090/metrics` - Prometheus format\n- `http://localhost:9090/health` - Health checks\n- `http://localhost:9090/status` - Detailed status\n\n### Query Optimizer Configuration (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"collect_statistics\": true,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Audit Logging Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"audit_logging\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"log_dir\": \"./audit_logs\",\n    \"max_size_mb\": 100,\n    \"max_age_days\": 30,\n    \"targets\": [\"file\", \"syslog\"],\n    \"exclude_commands\": [\"PING\"],\n    \"mask_commands\": [\"PASS\", \"PASSWORD\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### GPU Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8,\n    \"kernels\": [\"vector_ops\", \"matrix_mult\", \"sort\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\nSee [Configuration Guide](README_CONFIG.md) for complete documentation.\n\n## SQL Commands\n\n### Database Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create database\nCREATE DATABASE mydb;\n\n-- Use database\nUSE mydb;\n\n-- Drop database\nDROP DATABASE mydb;\n```\n\n### Table Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create table with constraints\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    email TEXT UNIQUE,\n    age INT CHECK (age >= 18),\n    metadata JSON,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Create table with foreign key\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    user_id INT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    total FLOAT CHECK (total > 0),\n    status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'shipped', 'delivered'))\n);\n\n-- Describe table\nDESCRIBE users;\n\n-- Drop table\nDROP TABLE users;\n```\n\n### ALTER TABLE (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Add column\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN phone TEXT;\n\n-- Add column with constraints\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive'));\n\n-- Drop column\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN phone;\n\n-- Drop column with CASCADE\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN email CASCADE;\n\n-- Modify column type\nALTER TABLE users MODIFY COLUMN age FLOAT;\n\n-- Rename column\nALTER TABLE users RENAME COLUMN name TO full_name;\n\n-- Add index\nALTER TABLE users ADD INDEX idx_email (email);\n\n-- Drop index\nALTER TABLE users DROP INDEX idx_email;\n\n-- Add foreign key constraint\nALTER TABLE orders ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id);\n\n-- Add CHECK constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT chk_age CHECK (age >= 18);\n\n-- Drop constraint\nALTER TABLE users DROP CONSTRAINT chk_age;\n```\n\n### Data Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Insert\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 30, '{\"city\": \"NYC\"}');\n\n-- Insert with JSON\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (2, 'Bob', 'bob@example.com', 25, '{\"city\": \"LA\", \"hobbies\": [\"reading\"]}');\n\n-- Select\nSELECT * FROM users;\nSELECT name, email FROM users WHERE age > 25;\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE name LIKE 'A%';\n\n-- JSON extraction\nSELECT name, metadata->city FROM users;\nSELECT name, metadata->>city FROM users;  -- As text\n\n-- Update\nUPDATE users SET age = 31 WHERE id = 1;\n\n-- Delete\nDELETE FROM users WHERE id = 1;\n```\n\n### Subqueries (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Scalar subquery\nSELECT name, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders) as order_count FROM users;\n\n-- IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders WHERE total > 100);\n\n-- NOT IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders);\n\n-- EXISTS subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders WHERE orders.user_id = users.id);\n\n-- Correlated subquery\nSELECT name, (SELECT MAX(total) FROM orders WHERE orders.user_id = users.id) as max_order\nFROM users;\n```\n\n### Views (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Create view\nCREATE VIEW active_users AS\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE status = 'active';\n\n-- Query view\nSELECT * FROM active_users WHERE age > 25;\n\n-- Drop view\nDROP VIEW active_users;\n\n-- Show views\nSHOW VIEWS;\n```\n\n### Full-Text Search (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Create full-text index\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles(content);\n\n-- Search with natural language mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database optimization');\n\n-- Search with boolean mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('+database -mysql' IN BOOLEAN MODE);\n\n-- Drop full-text index\nDROP FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles;\n```\n\n### User Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create user\nCREATE USER alice PASSWORD 'secret123';\n\n-- Grant privileges\nGRANT SELECT, INSERT ON mydb.users TO alice;\n\n-- Revoke privileges\nREVOKE DELETE ON mydb.users FROM alice;\n\n-- Show grants\nSHOW GRANTS FOR alice;\n```\n\n### Role Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create role\nCREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only access';\n\n-- Grant privileges to role\nGRANT SELECT ON *.* TO readonly;\n\n-- Assign role to user\nGRANT ROLE readonly TO alice;\n\n-- Show roles\nSHOW ROLES;\n```\n\n### Transactions\n\n```sql\n-- Begin transaction\nBEGIN TRANSACTION;\n\n-- Or simply\nBEGIN;\n\n-- Commit\nCOMMIT;\n\n-- Rollback\nROLLBACK;\n```\n\n### Backup Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Backup with encryption\nBACKUP DATABASE mydb TO /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword' COMPRESSION gzip;\n\n-- Restore with encryption\nRESTORE DATABASE mydb FROM /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword';\n```\n\n### Query Optimization (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Explain query plan\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\n\n-- Show plan cache status\nEXPLAIN CACHE;\n\n-- Analyze table for statistics\nANALYZE TABLE users;\n```\n\n## Environment Variables\n\nSensitive configuration values can be stored in environment variables:\n\n```bash\n# Encryption passphrase\nexport KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE=\"my-secret-key\"\n\n# TLS certificate password\nexport KOSDB_TLS_PASSWORD=\"cert-password\"\n\n# Backup encryption\nexport KOSDB_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE=\"backup-secret\"\n\n# JWT secret\nexport KOSDB_JWT_SECRET=\"jwt-signing-key\"\n```\n\nReference in config.json:\n```json\n{\n  \"database\": {\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Security Hardening\n\n### TLS Setup\n\n1. Generate CA and server certificates:\n```bash\n# Generate CA\nopenssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout ca.key -out ca.crt -days 365 -nodes\n\n# Generate server certificate\nopenssl req -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout server.key -out server.csr -nodes\nopenssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 365\n```\n\n2. Configure server:\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n3. Connect client with TLS:\n```bash\npython cli.py --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n### Encryption Best Practices\n\n1. **Use strong passphrases** (minimum 16 characters)\n2. **Store keys securely** (use key files with restricted permissions)\n3. **Rotate keys regularly** (use `ROTATE KEY` command)\n4. **Backup keys separately** from encrypted data\n5. **Enable audit logging** for encryption operations\n\n## Performance Tuning\n\n### GPU Acceleration\n\nEnable GPU for large-scale operations:\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8\n  }\n}\n```\n\nGPU-accelerated operations:\n- Vector mathematical operations\n- Matrix multiplication\n- Large dataset sorting\n- Aggregate functions\n\n### Query Plan Caching (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"invalidate_on_schema_change\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Connection Pooling\n\n```json\n{\n  \"performance\": {\n    \"connection_pool_min\": 5,\n    \"connection_pool_max\": 20,\n    \"query_cache_size\": 1000\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Health Check\n\n```bash\n# Check server health via HTTP\ncurl http://localhost:9090/health\n\n# Check via CLI\npython cli.py -c \"SHOW STATUS\"\n```\n\n### Metrics\n\nEnable Prometheus metrics:\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"prometheus_enabled\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\nAccess metrics:\n- `http://localhost:9090/metrics` - Prometheus format\n- `http://localhost:9090/health` - Health status\n- `http://localhost:9090/health/live` - Liveness probe\n- `http://localhost:9090/health/ready` - Readiness probe\n- `http://localhost:9090/status` - Detailed server status\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Issues\n\n- Verify server is running: `python cli.py -c \"PING\"`\n- Check firewall rules for port 9999\n- Verify TLS certificates are valid\n\n### Performance Issues\n\n- Check query cache hit rate: `EXPLAIN CACHE`\n- Monitor replication lag\n- Review slow query log\n- Check plan cache statistics\n\n### Encryption Issues\n\n- Verify passphrase is correct\n- Check key file permissions (should be 600)\n- Ensure cryptography library is installed\n\n## Migration from v3.1 to v3.2\n\nSee [MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md](MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md) for detailed migration guide.\n\n## API Reference\n\nSee [API Documentation](docs/API.md) for detailed command reference.\n\n## Contributing\n\nSee [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md) for contribution guidelines.\n\n## License\n\nMIT License -
