<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>CHANGELOG.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Changelog\n\nAll notable changes to KosDB will be documented in this file.\n\n## [3.2.0] - 2024-01-15\n\n### Added\n\n#### Query Optimization\n- **Query Plan Caching**: LRU cache for parsed execution plans with configurable size\n- **Cost-Based Optimizer**: Statistics-driven plan selection for better query performance\n- **Semi-Join Optimization**: Efficient IN/EXISTS subquery execution using semi-join transformation\n- **Index Advisor**: Automatic index recommendations based on query patterns\n- **Plan Cache Statistics**: Hit rate, miss rate, eviction tracking via EXPLAIN CACHE command\n\n#### Subquery Support\n- **Scalar Subqueries**: Support for (SELECT ...) in SELECT and WHERE clauses\n- **IN/NOT IN Subqueries**: Single column result subqueries with negation support\n- **EXISTS/NOT EXISTS Subqueries**: Correlated and non-correlated existence checks\n- **Correlated Subqueries**: Outer reference resolution for complex queries\n- **Semi-Join Transformation**: Query optimizer rewrites IN/EXISTS to semi-joins where applicable\n\n#### Advanced Constraints\n- **CHECK Constraints**: Data validation with complex expressions (=, !=, <, >, <=, >=, IN, BETWEEN, LIKE, IS NULL)\n- **Foreign Key Constraints**: Referential integrity with CASCADE, SET NULL, RESTRICT options\n- **Unique Constraints**: Multi-column unique constraints with automatic index creation\n\n#### ALTER TABLE Operations\n- **ADD COLUMN**: Add columns with full type support and constraints\n- **DROP COLUMN**: Remove columns with CASCADE handling for dependent objects\n- **MODIFY COLUMN**: Change column types with data validation\n- **RENAME COLUMN**: Rename existing columns with constraint updates\n- **ADD/DROP INDEX**: Dynamic index management\n- **ADD/DROP CONSTRAINT**: Foreign key, unique, and CHECK constraint management\n\n#### Views\n- **CREATE VIEW**: Virtual tables based on SELECT queries\n- **DROP VIEW**: View removal with dependency checking\n- **SHOW VIEWS**: List all views in database\n\n#### Full-Text Search\n- **MATCH ... AGAINST**: Natural language and boolean mode search\n- **Full-Text Indexes**: Inverted index for text search\n- **Relevance Scoring**: TF-IDF based result ranking\n- **Query Expansion**: Automatic synonym expansion\n\n#### JSON Support\n- **JSON Columns**: Native JSON data type storage\n- **JSON Extraction**: column->path and column->>path operators\n- **JSON Validation**: Automatic JSON format validation\n\n#### Monitoring and Metrics\n- **Prometheus Metrics**: Query counts, latency, cache hit rates, connection stats\n- **Health Endpoints**: /health, /health/live, /health/ready for container orchestration\n- **Status Endpoint**: /status for detailed server status\n- **Configurable Collection**: Metrics collection interval and retention settings\n\n#### SQL Enhancements\n- **EXPLAIN**: Query execution plan visualization\n- **EXPLAIN CACHE**: Plan cache status and statistics\n- **Transactions**: BEGIN, COMMIT, ROLLBACK support\n- **JSON Operators**: -> and ->> for JSON path extraction\n\n### Changed\n\n- **Parser**: Enhanced to support subqueries and complex WHERE clauses\n- **Query Optimizer**: Major rewrite with cost-based optimization\n- **Schema Storage**: Extended to support CHECK constraints and foreign keys\n- **Configuration**: New metrics and optimizer sections in config.json\n\n### Performance Improvements\n\n- Query plan caching reduces parsing overhead for repeated queries\n- Semi-join optimization improves IN/EXISTS subquery performance\n- Index recommendations help optimize query patterns\n- Connection metrics help identify bottlenecks\n\n### Deprecated\n\n- None\n\n### Removed\n\n- None\n\n### Security\n\n- Added privilege checks for ALTER TABLE operations\n- Constraint validation prevents data integrity violations\n- Foreign key enforcement maintains referential integrity\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- Fixed query parsing for complex nested conditions\n- Improved error messages for constraint violations\n- Fixed index updates during column modifications\n\n## [3.1.0] - 2023-12-01\n\n### Added\n\n#### Security Features\n- **TLS/SSL Encryption**: Certificate-based authentication and mTLS support\n- **At-Rest Encryption**: AES-256-GCM database encryption with PBKDF2\n- **Audit Logging**: Comprehensive operation logging with multiple targets\n- **Role-Based Access Control**: Granular permissions and role management\n\n#### Replication\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Automatic failover support\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multi-master with conflict resolution\n- **Async Replication**: Non-blocking replication\n\n#### Performance\n- **GPU Acceleration**: CUDA-powered query processing\n- **Connection Pooling**: Efficient connection management\n- **Query Caching**: Result cache for frequent queries\n\n#### Backup & Recovery\n- **Hot Backups**: Non-blocking encrypted backups\n- **Compression**: Multiple algorithms (gzip, lz4, zstd)\n- **Point-in-Time Recovery**: Restore to specific timestamp\n\n## [3.0.0] - 2023-10-15\n\n### Added\n\n- Initial release of KosDB\n- SQL-like interface with basic CRUD operations\n- Multiple database support\n- Primary and secondary indexing\n- User authentication and basic authorization\n- Binary logging for replication\n\n### Features\n\n- CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE operations\n- Multiple databases with USE command\n- Table schema with column types\n- Primary key and index support\n- Basic user management\n\n## Migration Notes\n\n### Upgrading to 3.2.0 from 3.1.0\n\n1. **Configuration Updates**:\n   - <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "Now let me create the migration guide:  <CreateFile>\n<fileName>MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Migration Guide: KosDB v3.1.0 to v3.2.0\n\nThis guide helps you upgrade from KosDB v3.1.0 to v3.2.0.\n\n## Overview\n\nKosDB v3.2.0 introduces significant new features including:\n- Query plan caching and optimization\n- Subquery support (IN, EXISTS, scalar)\n- CHECK constraints and foreign keys\n- ALTER TABLE operations\n- Views and full-text search\n- Prometheus metrics and monitoring\n- JSON data type support\n\n**Backward Compatibility**: v3.2.0 is fully backward compatible with v3.1.0. Existing databases will work without modification.\n\n## Quick Migration Steps\n\n### 1. Backup Your Data\n\n```bash\n# Create backup before upgrading\npython cli.py -c \"BACKUP DATABASE mydb TO /backups/pre-v3.2.backup\"\n```\n\n### 2. Update Configuration\n\nAdd new sections to your `config.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  \n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"collect_statistics\": true,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true\n  },\n  \n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15,\n    \"retention_days\": 30,\n    \"endpoints\": {\n      \"metrics\": \"/metrics\",\n      \"health\": \"/health\",\n      \"status\": \"/status\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Update Dependencies\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n### 4. Restart Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py -c config.json\n```\n\n### 5. Verify Upgrade\n\n```bash\n# Check version\npython cli.py -c \"SELECT version()\"\n\n# Test new features\npython cli.py -c \"EXPLAIN CACHE\"\n```\n\n## Detailed Migration\n\n### Configuration Changes\n\n#### New Required Sections\n\n**Optimizer Configuration** (required for query optimization):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"collect_statistics\": true,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true,\n    \"statistics_ttl\": 3600\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Description | Default |\n|--------|-------------|---------|\n| `enabled` | Enable query optimizer | `true` |\n| `cache_size` | Number of cached execution plans | `100` |\n| `collect_statistics` | Auto-collect table statistics | `true` |\n| `enable_semi_join` | Optimize IN/EXISTS with semi-join | `true` |\n| `statistics_ttl` | Statistics cache TTL in seconds | `3600` |\n\n**Metrics Configuration** (optional, for monitoring):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15,\n    \"retention_days\": 30\n  }\n}\n```\n\n#### Deprecated Options\n\nNone. All v3.1.0 configuration options remain valid.\n\n### Database Schema Changes\n\n#### Adding CHECK Constraints\n\nExisting tables can have CHECK constraints added:\n\n```sql\n-- Add CHECK constraint to existing table\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT chk_age CHECK (age >= 18);\n\n-- Add column with CHECK constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive'));\n```\n\n**Note**: CHECK constraints only apply to new INSERT/UPDATE operations. Existing data is not validated.\n\n#### Adding Foreign Keys\n\nForeign keys can be added to existing tables:\n\n```sql\n-- Add foreign key constraint\nALTER TABLE orders ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user \n  FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;\n```\n\n**Note**: Foreign key constraints are enforced immediately. Ensure existing data satisfies the constraint before adding.\n\n#### Creating Views\n\nViews provide a way to create virtual tables:\n\n```sql\n-- Create view from existing data\nCREATE VIEW active_users AS \nSELECT * FROM users WHERE status = 'active';\n\n-- Query view like a table\nSELECT * FROM active_users WHERE age > 25;\n```\n\n### SQL Syntax Changes\n\n#### New Statements\n\n**Subqueries**:\n\n```sql\n-- Scalar subquery\nSELECT name, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders) FROM users;\n\n-- IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders);\n\n-- EXISTS subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders WHERE user_id = users.id);\n```\n\n**ALTER TABLE**:\n\n```sql\n-- Add column\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN email TEXT;\n\n-- Modify column\nALTER TABLE users MODIFY COLUMN age FLOAT;\n\n-- Rename column\nALTER TABLE users RENAME COLUMN name TO full_name;\n\n-- Drop column\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN email CASCADE;\n\n-- Add index\nALTER TABLE users ADD INDEX idx_name (name);\n\n-- Add constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT chk_age CHECK (age >= 0);\n```\n\n**JSON Operations**:\n\n```sql\n-- Create table with JSON column\nCREATE TABLE events (id INT, data JSON);\n\n-- Insert JSON data\nINSERT INTO events VALUES (1, '{\"type\": \"click\", \"x\": 100, \"y\": 200}');\n\n-- Query with JSON extraction\nSELECT data->type, data->>x FROM events;\n```\n\n**Full-Text Search**:\n\n```sql\n-- Create full-text index\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles(content);\n\n-- Search\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database');\n```\n\n**EXPLAIN**:\n\n```sql\n-- Show query plan\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\n\n-- Show cache status\nEXPLAIN CACHE;\n```\n\n### Privilege Changes\n\n#### New Privileges\n\nv3.2.0 adds new privilege types:\n\n| Privilege | Description |\n|-----------|-------------|\n| `ALTER` | ALTER TABLE operations |\n| `REFERENCES` | Create foreign keys |\n| `INDEX` | Create/drop indexes |\n\n#### Updating User Privileges\n\nGrant new privileges to existing users:\n\n```sql\n-- Grant ALTER privilege\nGRANT ALTER ON mydb.* TO admin;\n\n-- Grant REFERENCES for foreign keys\nGRANT REFERENCES ON mydb.* TO developer;\n\n-- Grant INDEX privilege\nGRANT INDEX ON mydb.* TO developer;\n```\n\n### Monitoring Setup\n\n#### Prometheus Integration\n\n1. **Enable metrics endpoint**:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090\n  }\n}\n```\n\n2. **Configure Prometheus** (prometheus.yml):\n\n```yaml\nscrape_configs:\n  - job_name: 'kosdb'\n    static_configs:\n      - targets: ['localhost:9090']\n    metrics_path: /metrics\n```\n\n3. **Health checks for Kubernetes**:\n\n```yaml\nlivenessProbe:\n  httpGet:\n    path: /health/live\n    port: 9090\n  initialDelaySeconds: 30\n  periodSeconds: 10\n\nreadinessProbe:\n  httpGet:\n    path: /health/ready\n    port: 9090\n  initialDelaySeconds: 5\n  periodSeconds: 5\n```\n\n### Performance Considerations\n\n#### Query Plan Cache\n\nThe query plan cache improves performance for repeated queries:\n\n```sql\n-- Check cache statistics\nEXPLAIN CACHE;\n\n-- Typical output:\n-- Plan Cache Status:\n-- Size: 45 / 100 entries\n-- Hit Rate: 87.5%\n-- Total Hits: 350\n-- Total Misses: 50\n```\n\n**Tuning**:\n- Increase `cache_size` for high query diversity workloads\n- Decrease for memory-constrained environments\n\n#### Statistics Collection\n\nAutomatic statistics collection helps the optimizer:\n\n```sql\n-- Trigger statistics update\nANALYZE TABLE users;\n\n-- Check statistics (via EXPLAIN)\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\n```\n\n### Troubleshooting\n\n#### Migration Issues\n\n**Issue**: \"Unknown configuration option 'optimizer'\"\n\n**Solution**: Update config.json version to \"3.2.0\":\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n**Issue**: \"ALTER TABLE not supported\"\n\n**Solution**: Ensure you're running v3.2.0:\n\n```bash\npython server.py --version\n# Should show: KosDB v3.2.0\n```\n\n**Issue**: \"Subquery syntax error\"\n\n**Solution**: Verify parser is updated. Check that subqueries use correct syntax:\n\n```sql\n-- Correct\nSELECT * FROM t1 WHERE id IN (SELECT id FROM t2);\n\n-- Incorrect (missing parentheses)\nSELECT * FROM t1 WHERE id IN SELECT id FROM t2;\n```\n\n#### Performance Regression\n\nIf queries are slower after upgrade:\n\n1. **Check plan cache hit rate**:\n   ```sql\n   EXPLAIN CACHE;\n   ```\n\n2. **Analyze tables**:\n   ```sql\n   ANALYZE TABLE users;\n   ANALYZE TABLE orders;\n   ```\n\n3. **Disable semi-join optimization** (if causing issues):\n   ```json\n   {\n     \"optimizer\": {\n       \"enable_semi_join\": false\n     }\n   }\n   ```\n\n### Rollback Procedure\n\nIf you need to rollback to v3.1.0:\n\n1. **Stop v3.2.0 server**\n\n2. **Restore v3.1.0 code**:\n   ```bash\n   git checkout v3.1.0\n   ```\n\n3. **Restore config.json** (remove optimizer and metrics sections)\n\n4. **Restart server**\n\n**Note**: Databases created with v3.2.0-specific features (CHECK constraints, views) will still work in v3.1.0, but those features won't be accessible.\n\n## Feature Adoption Guide\n\n### Phase 1: Basic Upgrade (Week 1)\n- Update configuration\n- Verify existing functionality\n- Enable metrics endpoint\n\n### Phase 2: Optimization (Week 2-3)\n- Monitor query plan cache hit rates\n- Add recommended indexes\n- Analyze slow queries with EXPLAIN\n\n### Phase 3: New Features (Week 4+)\n- Add CHECK constraints to new <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>README_CONFIG.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># KosDB Configuration Guide\n\nComplete reference for KosDB configuration options.\n\n## Configuration File Structure\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  \"server\": { ... },\n  \"database\": { ... },\n  \"tls\": { ... },\n  \"security\": { ... },\n  \"authentication\": { ... },\n  \"authorization\": { ... },\n  \"replication\": { ... },\n  \"audit_logging\": { ... },\n  \"performance\": { ... },\n  \"gpu\": { ... },\n  \"optimizer\": { ... },\n  \"metrics\": { ... },\n  \"monitoring\": { ... },\n  \"backup\": { ... }\n}\n```\n\n## Core Settings\n\n### version\n- **Type**: string\n- **Required**: Yes\n- **Description**: Configuration version. Must match server version.\n- **Example**: `\"3.2.0\"`\n\n### server\n\nServer network and connection settings.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9999,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\",\n    \"max_connections\": 100,\n    \"connection_timeout\": 300,\n    \"request_timeout\": 60\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `host` | string | `\"0.0.0.0\"` | Bind address |\n| `port` | int | `9999` | TCP port |\n| `data_dir` | string | `\"./data\"` | Database files directory |\n| `max_connections` | int | `100` | Maximum concurrent connections |\n| `connection_timeout` | int | `300` | Connection idle timeout (seconds) |\n| `request_timeout` | int | `60` | Request processing timeout (seconds) |\n\n### database\n\nDatabase engine and storage settings.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"database\": {\n    \"engine\": \"leveldb\",\n    \"compression\": true,\n    \"compression_algorithm\": \"snappy\",\n    \"cache_size_mb\": 256,\n    \"write_buffer_mb\": 64,\n    \"max_open_files\": 1000,\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"enabled\": false,\n      \"algorithm\": \"AES-256-GCM\",\n      \"key_derivation\": \"PBKDF2\",\n      \"iterations\": 100000,\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `engine` | string | `\"leveldb\"` | Storage engine (leveldb) |\n| `compression` | bool | `true` | Enable compression |\n| `compression_algorithm` | string | `\"snappy\"` | Compression type (snappy, zlib) |\n| `cache_size_mb` | int | `256` | Block cache size |\n| `write_buffer_mb` | int | `64` | Write buffer size |\n| `max_open_files` | int | `1000` | Maximum open file handles |\n\n#### Encryption Settings\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `false` | Enable at-rest encryption |\n| `algorithm` | string | `\"AES-256-GCM\"` | Encryption algorithm |\n| `key_derivation` | string | `\"PBKDF2\"` | Key derivation function |\n| `iterations` | int | `100000` | PBKDF2 iterations |\n| `passphrase` | string | - | Encryption passphrase (use env var) |\n| `passphrase_env` | string | - | Environment variable for passphrase |\n| `key_file` | string | - | Path to key file |\n\n## Security Settings\n\n### tls\n\nTLS/SSL configuration.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": false,\n    \"cert_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": false,\n    \"protocols\": [\"TLSv1.2\", \"TLSv1.3\"],\n    \"ciphers\": \"HIGH:!aNULL:!MD5\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `false` | Enable TLS |\n| `cert_file` | string | - | Server certificate file |\n| `key_file` | string | - | Server private key file |\n| `ca_file` | string | - | CA certificate file |\n| `client_auth` | bool | `false` | Require client certificates |\n| `protocols` | array | `[\"TLSv1.2\", \"TLSv1.3\"]` | Allowed TLS versions |\n| `ciphers` | string | `\"HIGH:!aNULL:!MD5\"` | Cipher suite selection |\n\n### security\n\nGeneral security settings.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"security\": {\n    \"require_authentication\": true,\n    \"min_password_length\": 8,\n    \"password_hash_algorithm\": \"bcrypt\",\n    \"password_hash_rounds\": 12,\n    \"session_timeout\": 3600,\n    \"max_failed_logins\": 5,\n    \"lockout_duration\": 300\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `require_authentication` | bool | `true` | Require login |\n| `min_password_length` | int | `8` | Minimum password length |\n| `password_hash_algorithm` | string | `\"bcrypt\"` | Hash algorithm |\n| `password_hash_rounds` | int | `12` | Bcrypt cost factor |\n| `session_timeout` | int | `3600` | Session TTL (seconds) |\n| `max_failed_logins` | int | `5` | Failed attempts before lockout |\n| `lockout_duration` | int | `300` | Account lockout duration |\n\n## Authentication & Authorization\n\n### authentication\n\nAuthentication methods configuration.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"authentication\": {\n    \"methods\": [\"password\", \"jwt\"],\n    \"jwt\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"secret_env\": \"KOSDB_JWT_SECRET\",\n      \"algorithm\": \"HS256\",\n      \"expiration\": 3600\n    },\n    \"ldap\": {\n      \"enabled\": false,\n      \"server\": \"ldap://localhost:389\",\n      \"bind_dn\": \"cn=admin,dc=example,dc=com\",\n      \"base_dn\": \"dc=example,dc=com\",\n      \"user_filter\": \"(uid={username})\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### authorization\n\nRBAC configuration.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"authorization\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"default_role\": \"readonly\",\n    \"cache_ttl\": 300,\n    \"column_level_security\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Replication Settings\n\n### replication\n\nMaster-slave and master-master replication.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"replication\": {\n    \"enabled\": false,\n    \"role\": \"master\",\n    \"server_id\": 1,\n    \"binlog\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"format\": \"row\",\n      \"retention_days\": 7\n    },\n    \"slaves\": [\n      {\n        \"host\": \"slave1.example.com\",\n        \"port\": 9999,\n        \"user\": \"replica\",\n        \"password_env\": \"REPLICA_PASSWORD\"\n      }\n    ],\n    \"master\": {\n      \"host\": \"master.example.com\",\n      \"port\": 9999,\n      \"user\": \"replica\",\n      \"password_env\": \"REPLICA_PASSWORD\"\n    },\n    \"sync_replication\": false,\n    \"replication_timeout\": 30\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `false` | Enable replication |\n| `role` | string | `\"master\"` | Server role (master/slave) |\n| `server_id` | int | `1` | Unique server ID |\n| `sync_replication` | bool | `false` | Synchronous replication |\n| `replication_timeout` | int | `30` | Replication timeout (seconds) |\n\n## Audit Logging\n\n### audit_logging\n\nComprehensive operation logging.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"audit_logging\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"log_dir\": \"./audit_logs\",\n    \"log_format\": \"json\",\n    \"max_size_mb\": 100,\n    \"max_age_days\": 30,\n    \"max_backups\": 10,\n    \"compress_backups\": true,\n    \"targets\": [\"file\", \"syslog\"],\n    \"syslog\": {\n      \"address\": \"localhost:514\",\n      \"protocol\": \"udp\",\n      \"facility\": \"local0\"\n    },\n    \"webhook\": {\n      \"url\": \"https://logs.example.com/webhook\",\n      \"headers\": {\n        \"Authorization\": \"Bearer token\"\n      }\n    },\n    \"log_commands\": [\"SELECT\", \"INSERT\", \"UPDATE\", \"DELETE\"],\n    \"exclude_commands\": [\"PING\", \"SHOW STATUS\"],\n    \"mask_commands\": [\"CREATE USER\", \"ALTER USER\"],\n    \"mask_fields\": [\"password\", \"secret\", \"token\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `true` | Enable audit logging |\n| `log_dir` | string | `\"./audit_logs\"` | Log file directory |\n| `log_format` | string | `\"json\"` | Log format (json/csv) |\n| `max_size_mb` | int | `100` | Max log file size |\n| `max_age_days` | int | `30` | Log retention |\n| `targets` | array | `[\"file\"]` | Output targets |\n\n## Performance Settings\n\n### performance\n\nQuery execution and caching.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"performance\": {\n    \"query_cache\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"size_mb\": 64,\n      \"ttl_seconds\": 300\n    },\n    \"connection_pool\": {\n      \"min_size\": 5,\n      \"max_size\": 20,\n      \"max_idle_time\": 300\n    },\n    \"parallel_execution\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"max_workers\": 4,\n      \"min_rows_for_parallel\": 10000\n    },\n    \"slow_query_threshold_ms\": 1000,\n    \"log_slow_queries\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `query_cache.enabled` | bool | `true` | Enable result caching |\n| `query_cache.size_mb` | int | `64` | Cache size |\n| `slow_query_threshold_ms` | int | `1000` | Slow query threshold |\n\n## GPU Acceleration\n\n### gpu\n\nCUDA GPU acceleration settings.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": false,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8,\n    \"kernels\": [\"vector_ops\", \"matrix_mult\", \"sort\"],\n    \"min_rows_for_gpu\": 10000,\n    \"batch_size\": 1024\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `false` | Enable GPU |\n| `device_id` | int | `0` | CUDA device ID |\n| `memory_fraction` | float | `0.8` | GPU memory fraction |\n| `min_rows_for_gpu` | int | `10000` | Minimum rows for GPU |\n\n## Query Optimizer (New in v3.2.0)\n\n### optimizer\n\nQuery plan caching and optimization.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"collect_statistics\": true,\n    \"statistics_ttl\": 3600,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true,\n    \"enable_index_advisor\": true,\n    \"cost_model\": \"hybrid\",\n    \"plan_cache\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"max_size\": 100,\n      \"eviction_policy\": \"lru\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `true` | Enable optimizer |\n| `cache_size` | int | `100` | Plan cache entries |\n| `collect_statistics` | bool | `true` | Auto-collect statistics |\n| `statistics_ttl` | int | `3600` | Statistics TTL (seconds) |\n| `enable_semi_join` | bool | `true` | Semi-join optimization |\n| `enable_index_advisor` | bool | `true` | Index recommendations |\n| `cost_model` | string | `\"hybrid\"` | Cost model type |\n\n## Metrics and Monitoring (New in v3.2.0)\n\n### metrics\n\nPrometheus-compatible metrics.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15,\n    \"retention_days\": 30,\n    \"endpoints\": {\n      \"metrics\": \"/metrics\",\n      \"health\": \"/health\",\n      \"status\": \"/status\"\n    },\n    \"collectors\": {\n      \"query_metrics\": true,\n      \"cache_metrics\": true,\n      \"connection_metrics\": true,\n      \"replication_metrics\": true,\n      \"storage_metrics\": true\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `true` | Enable metrics |\n| `host` | string | `\"0.0.0.0\"` | Bind address |\n| `port` | int | `9090` | HTTP port |\n| `collection_interval` | int | `15` | Collection interval (seconds) |\n| `retention_days` | int | `30` | Data retention |\n\n### monitoring\n\nHealth monitoring and alerts.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"monitoring\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"health_check_interval\": 30,\n    \"slow_query_threshold_ms\": 1000,\n    \"alert_webhook\": \"https://alerts.example.com/webhook\",\n    \"metrics_retention_hours\": 168\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Backup Settings\n\n### backup\n\nBackup and recovery configuration.\n\n```json\n{\n  \"backup\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"backup_dir\": \"./backups\",\n    \"schedule\": \"0 2 * * *\",\n    \"retention_count\": 7,\n    \"compression\": \"gzip\",\n    \"compression_level\": 6,\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"algorithm\": \"AES-256-GCM\",\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE\"\n    },\n    \"verify_backups\": true,\n    \"notify_on_failure\": true,\n    \"notification_email\": \"admin@example.com\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Option | Type | Default | Description |\n|--------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `enabled` | bool | `true` | Enable scheduled backups |\n| `schedule` | string | `\"0 2 * * *\"` | Cron schedule |\n| `retention_count` | int | `7` | Backup retention count |\n| `compression` | string | `\"gzip\"` | Compression algorithm |\n| `verify_backups` | bool | `true` | Verify after backup |\n\n## Environment Variables\n\nSensitive values should use environment variables:\n\n| Variable | Description | Used In |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE` | Database encryption key | `database.encryption` |\n| `KOSDB_TLS_PASSWORD` | TLS key password | `tls` |\n| `KOSDB_JWT_SECRET` | JWT signing key | `authentication.jwt` |\n| `KOSDB_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE` | Backup encryption key | `backup.encryption` |\n| `KOSDB_ADMIN_PASSWORD` | Initial admin password | Setup |\n\n## Complete Example Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9999,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\",\n    \"max_connections\": 100\n  },\n  \"database\": {\n    \"engine\": \"leveldb\",\n    \"compression\": true,\n    \"cache_size_mb\": 256,\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE\"\n    }\n  },\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.key\",\n    \"client_auth\": false\n  },\n  \"security\": {\n    \"require_authentication\": true,\n    \"min_password_length\": 12\n  },\n  \"audit_logging\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"log_dir\": \"./audit_logs\",\n    \"max_size_mb\": 100,\n    \"targets\": [\"file\"]\n  },\n  \"performance\": {\n    \"query_cache\": {\n      \"enabled\": true,\n      \"size_mb\": 64\n    }\n  },\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true\n  },\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15\n  },\n  \"backup\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"backup_dir\": \"./backups\",\n    \"schedule\": \"0 2 * * *\",\n    \"retention_count\": 7\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Validation\n\nValidate your configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Start server with config validation\npython server.py -c config.json --validate\n\n# Test configuration without starting server\npython server.py -c config.json --check-config\n```\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Configuration Errors\n\n**\"Unknown configuration option\"**\n- Check `version` matches server version\n- Verify option name spelling\n- See this guide for valid options\n\n**\"Invalid value for option\"**\n- Check data type (string, int, bool, array)\n- Verify enum values are valid\n- Ensure file paths exist\n\n**\"Missing required option\"**\n- Check all required sections are present\n- Verify `version` is set\n- Ensure `server.data_dir` exists\n\n### Performance Issues\n\n**High memory usage**\n- Reduce `database.cache_size_mb`\n- Lower `optimizer.cache_size`\n- Decrease `performance.query_cache.size_mb`\n\n**Slow queries**\n- Enable `optimizer.collect_statistics`\n- Increase `database.cache_size_mb`\n- Check `optimizer.enable_semi_join` is true\n</contentOfFile>\n</WriteFile>", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 42, "timestamp": 1783744283.0794835, "date": "2026-07-11", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 122717, "response_tokens": 4031} -->

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>docs/SQL_REFERENCE.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># KosDB SQL Reference\n\nComplete SQL syntax reference for KosDB v3.2.0.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Data Types](#data-types)\n- [DDL Commands](#ddl-commands)\n- [DML Commands](#dml-commands)\n- [DCL Commands](#dcl-commands)\n- [TCL Commands](#tcl-commands)\n- [Query Operations](#query-operations)\n- [Functions](#functions)\n- [Constraints](#constraints)\n- [Operators](#operators)\n\n## Data Types\n\n| Type | Description | Example |\n|------|-------------|---------|\n| `INT` | 64-bit integer | `42` |\n| `FLOAT` | Double-precision float | `3.14` |\n| `TEXT` | Variable-length string | `'Hello'` |\n| `BOOLEAN` | True/False value | `TRUE`, `FALSE` |\n| `JSON` | JSON document | `'{\"key\": \"value\"}'` |\n| `BLOB` | Binary data | `X'1A2B3C'` |\n| `TIMESTAMP` | Date and time | `'2024-01-15 10:30:00'` |\n\n## DDL Commands\n\n### CREATE DATABASE\n\nCreate a new database.\n\n```sql\nCREATE DATABASE database_name;\n```\n\n### DROP DATABASE\n\nDelete a database.\n\n```sql\nDROP DATABASE database_name;\n```\n\n### USE\n\nSelect current database.\n\n```sql\nUSE database_name;\n```\n\n### CREATE TABLE\n\nCreate a new table with columns and constraints.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE table_name (\n    column_name data_type [constraints],\n    ...\n    [table_constraints]\n);\n```\n\n**Example:**\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    email TEXT UNIQUE,\n    age INT CHECK (age >= 18),\n    metadata JSON,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    \n    -- Table-level constraints\n    CONSTRAINT chk_email CHECK (email LIKE '%@%'),\n    INDEX idx_name (name)\n);\n```\n\n### DROP TABLE\n\nDelete a table.\n\n```sql\nDROP TABLE table_name;\n```\n\n### ALTER TABLE\n\nModify table structure (v3.2.0+).\n\n#### ADD COLUMN\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name ADD COLUMN column_name data_type [constraints];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN phone TEXT;\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive'));\n```\n\n#### DROP COLUMN\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name DROP COLUMN column_name [CASCADE];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN phone;\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN email CASCADE;\n```\n\n#### MODIFY COLUMN\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name MODIFY COLUMN column_name new_data_type [constraints];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users MODIFY COLUMN age FLOAT;\n```\n\n#### RENAME COLUMN\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name RENAME COLUMN old_name TO new_name;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users RENAME COLUMN name TO full_name;\n```\n\n#### ADD INDEX\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name ADD INDEX index_name (column1, column2, ...);\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users ADD INDEX idx_email (email);\nALTER TABLE users ADD INDEX idx_name_age (name, age);\n```\n\n#### DROP INDEX\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name DROP INDEX index_name;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users DROP INDEX idx_email;\n```\n\n#### ADD CONSTRAINT\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name ADD CONSTRAINT constraint_name constraint_definition;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\n-- Foreign key\nALTER TABLE orders ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user \n    FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE;\n\n-- CHECK constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT chk_age CHECK (age >= 0);\n\n-- UNIQUE constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT uk_email UNIQUE (email);\n```\n\n#### DROP CONSTRAINT\n\n```sql\nALTER TABLE table_name DROP CONSTRAINT constraint_name;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nALTER TABLE users DROP CONSTRAINT chk_age;\n```\n\n### CREATE VIEW\n\nCreate a virtual table based on a query (v3.2.0+).\n\n```sql\nCREATE VIEW view_name AS select_statement;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nCREATE VIEW active_users AS\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE status = 'active';\n\nCREATE VIEW user_orders AS\nSELECT u.name, o.total, o.status\nFROM users u\nJOIN orders o ON u.id = o.user_id;\n```\n\n### DROP VIEW\n\nDelete a view.\n\n```sql\nDROP VIEW view_name;\n```\n\n### CREATE FULLTEXT INDEX\n\nCreate full-text search index (v3.2.0+).\n\n```sql\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX index_name ON table_name(column_name);\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles(content);\n```\n\n### DROP FULLTEXT INDEX\n\nRemove full-text index.\n\n```sql\nDROP FULLTEXT INDEX index_name ON table_name;\n```\n\n## DML Commands\n\n### INSERT\n\nInsert data into a table.\n\n```sql\nINSERT INTO table_name VALUES (value1, value2, ...);\nINSERT INTO table_name (column1, column2) VALUES (value1, value2);\nINSERT INTO table_name VALUES (value1, value2, ...), (value3, value4, ...);\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 30, NULL);\nINSERT INTO users (name, email) VALUES ('Bob', 'bob@example.com');\nINSERT INTO users VALUES \n    (2, 'Charlie', 'charlie@example.com', 25, NULL),\n    (3, 'Diana', 'diana@example.com', 28, NULL);\n```\n\n### SELECT\n\nQuery data from tables.\n\n```sql\nSELECT [DISTINCT] column1, column2, ...\nFROM table_name\n[JOIN ...]\n[WHERE conditions]\n[GROUP BY column1, ...]\n[HAVING conditions]\n[ORDER BY column1 [ASC|DESC], ...]\n[LIMIT n [OFFSET m]];\n```\n\n**Basic Examples:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users;\nSELECT name, email FROM users;\nSELECT DISTINCT status FROM users;\n```\n\n#### WHERE Clause\n\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE name = 'Alice';\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE email LIKE '%@example.com';\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE age BETWEEN 20 AND 30;\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE status IN ('active', 'pending');\n```\n\n#### JOIN Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Inner join\nSELECT * FROM users u JOIN orders o ON u.id = o.user_id;\n\n-- Left join\nSELECT * FROM users u LEFT JOIN orders o ON u.id = o.user_id;\n\n-- Multiple joins\nSELECT * FROM users u\nJOIN orders o ON u.id = o.user_id\nJOIN products p ON o.product_id = p.id;\n```\n\n#### Subqueries (v3.2.0+)\n\n**Scalar Subquery:**\n```sql\nSELECT name, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders) as order_count \nFROM users;\n```\n\n**IN Subquery:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders WHERE total > 100);\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders);\n```\n\n**EXISTS Subquery:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders WHERE user_id = users.id);\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders WHERE user_id = users.id);\n```\n\n**Correlated Subquery:**\n```sql\nSELECT name, \n    (SELECT MAX(total) FROM orders WHERE orders.user_id = users.id) as max_order\nFROM users;\n```\n\n#### JSON Operations (v3.2.0+)\n\n```sql\n-- Extract JSON value\nSELECT metadata->city FROM users;\nSELECT metadata->>'city' FROM users;  -- As text\n\n-- Filter by JSON value\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE metadata->type = 'premium';\n```\n\n#### Full-Text Search (v3.2.0+)\n\n```sql\n-- Natural language mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database optimization');\n\n-- Boolean mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('+database -mysql' IN BOOLEAN MODE);\n\n-- With query expansion\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database' WITH QUERY EXPANSION);\n```\n\n#### ORDER BY\n\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users ORDER BY age;\nSELECT * FROM users ORDER BY age DESC;\nSELECT * FROM users ORDER BY name ASC, age DESC;\n```\n\n#### LIMIT and OFFSET\n\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM users LIMIT 10;\nSELECT * FROM users LIMIT 10 OFFSET 20;\nSELECT * FROM users ORDER BY id LIMIT 10 OFFSET 20;\n```\n\n### UPDATE\n\nModify existing data.\n\n```sql\nUPDATE table_name \nSET column1 = value1, column2 = value2, ...\n[WHERE conditions];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nUPDATE users SET age = 31 WHERE id = 1;\nUPDATE users SET status = 'inactive', updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP \nWHERE last_login < '2023-01-01';\nUPDATE users SET metadata = '{\"tier\": \"premium\"}' WHERE id = 1;\n```\n\n### DELETE\n\nRemove data from tables.\n\n```sql\nDELETE FROM table_name [WHERE conditions];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nDELETE FROM users WHERE id = 1;\nDELETE FROM users WHERE status = 'inactive';\nDELETE FROM users;  -- Delete all rows (use with caution!)\n```\n\n## DCL Commands\n\n### CREATE USER\n\nCreate a new database user.\n\n```sql\nCREATE USER username PASSWORD 'password';\n```\n\n### DROP USER\n\nDelete a user.\n\n```sql\nDROP USER username;\n```\n\n### GRANT\n\nGrant privileges to users or roles.\n\n```sql\nGRANT privilege_list ON database.table TO username;\nGRANT privilege_list ON database.* TO username;\nGRANT privilege_list ON *.* TO username;\n```\n\n**Privileges:** SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, DROP, ALTER, INDEX, REFERENCES, ADMIN\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nGRANT SELECT, INSERT ON mydb.users TO alice;\nGRANT ALL ON mydb.* TO admin;\nGRANT REFERENCES ON mydb.* TO developer;\n```\n\n### REVOKE\n\nRemove privileges.\n\n```sql\nREVOKE privilege_list ON database.table FROM username;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nREVOKE DELETE ON mydb.users FROM alice;\nREVOKE ALL ON mydb.* FROM admin;\n```\n\n### CREATE ROLE\n\nCreate a role (v3.2.0+).\n\n```sql\nCREATE ROLE role_name [DESCRIPTION 'description'];\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nCREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only database access';\nCREATE ROLE developer DESCRIPTION 'Full development access';\n```\n\n### DROP ROLE\n\nDelete a role.\n\n```sql\nDROP ROLE role_name;\n```\n\n### GRANT ROLE\n\nAssign role to user.\n\n```sql\nGRANT ROLE role_name TO username;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nGRANT ROLE readonly TO alice;\n```\n\n### REVOKE ROLE\n\nRemove role from user.\n\n```sql\nREVOKE ROLE role_name FROM username;\n```\n\n### SHOW GRANTS\n\nDisplay user privileges.\n\n```sql\nSHOW GRANTS [FOR username];\n```\n\n## TCL Commands\n\n### BEGIN\n\nStart a transaction.\n\n```sql\nBEGIN [TRANSACTION];\n```\n\n### COMMIT\n\nCommit transaction.\n\n```sql\nCOMMIT;\n```\n\n### ROLLBACK\n\nRollback transaction.\n\n```sql\nROLLBACK;\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nBEGIN;\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com');\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (1, 1, 100.00);\nCOMMIT;\n```\n\n## Query Operations\n\n### EXPLAIN\n\nShow query execution plan (v3.2.0+).\n\n```sql\nEXPLAIN select_statement;\nEXPLAIN CACHE;  -- Show plan cache statistics\n```\n\n**Example:**\n```sql\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE id IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders);\n```\n\n### ANALYZE\n\nUpdate table statistics.\n\n```sql\nANALYZE TABLE table_name;\n```\n\n### DESCRIBE\n\nShow table structure.\n\n```sql\nDESCRIBE table_name;\n```\n\n### SHOW\n\nDisplay database information.\n\n```sql\nSHOW DATABASES;\nSHOW TABLES;\nSHOW USERS;\nSHOW VIEWS;  -- v3.2.0+\nSHOW ROLES;   -- v3.2.0+\nSHOW GRANTS [FOR username];\n```\n\n## Functions\n\n### Aggregate Functions\n\n| Function | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `COUNT(*)` | Count rows | `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users` |\n| `COUNT(column)` | Count non-null | `SELECT COUNT(email) FROM users` |\n| `SUM(column)` | Sum values | `SELECT SUM(total) FROM orders` |\n| `AVG(column)` | Average | `SELECT AVG(age) FROM users` |\n| `MIN(column)` | Minimum | `SELECT MIN(age) FROM users` |\n| `MAX(column)` | Maximum | `SELECT MAX(age) FROM users` |\n\n### String Functions\n\n| Function | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `CONCAT(s1, s2)` | Concatenate | `SELECT CONCAT(first_name, ' ', last_name)` |\n| `UPPER(s)` | Uppercase | `SELECT UPPER(name) FROM users` |\n| `LOWER(s)` | Lowercase | `SELECT LOWER(email) FROM users` |\n| `LENGTH(s)` | String length | `SELECT LENGTH(name) FROM users` |\n| `SUBSTRING(s, start, len)` | Extract substring | `SELECT SUBSTRING(name, 1, 3)` |\n| `TRIM(s)` | Remove whitespace | `SELECT TRIM(name) FROM users` |\n\n### Numeric Functions\n\n| Function | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `ABS(n)` | Absolute value | `SELECT ABS(-10)` |\n| `ROUND(n, d)` | Round to d decimals | `SELECT ROUND(3.14159, 2)` |\n| `CEIL(n)` | Round up | `SELECT CEIL(3.2)` |\n| `FLOOR(n)` | Round down | `SELECT FLOOR(3.8)` |\n| `MOD(n, m)` | Modulo | `SELECT MOD(10, 3)` |\n\n### Date/Time Functions\n\n| Function | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `CURRENT_TIMESTAMP` | Current datetime | `SELECT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP` |\n| `NOW()` | Current datetime | `SELECT NOW()` |\n| `DATE(timestamp)` | Extract date | `SELECT DATE(created_at)` |\n| `YEAR(timestamp)` | Extract year | `SELECT YEAR(created_at)` |\n| `MONTH(timestamp)` | Extract month | `SELECT MONTH(created_at)` |\n| `DAY(timestamp)` | Extract day | `SELECT DAY(created_at)` |\n\n### JSON Functions (v3.2.0+)\n\n| Function | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `JSON_EXTRACT(json, path)` | Extract value | `SELECT JSON_EXTRACT(metadata, '$.city')` |\n| `JSON_EXTRACT_TEXT(json, path)` | Extract as text | `SELECT JSON_EXTRACT_TEXT(metadata, '$.city')` |\n\n## Constraints\n\n### PRIMARY KEY\n\nUnique identifier for rows.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    ...\n);\n```\n\n### UNIQUE\n\nEnsure column values are unique.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    email TEXT UNIQUE,\n    ...\n);\n\n-- Multi-column unique\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    user_id INT,\n    order_number INT,\n    UNIQUE (user_id, order_number)\n);\n```\n\n### NOT NULL\n\nRequire non-null values.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    ...\n);\n```\n\n### CHECK (v3.2.0+)\n\nValidate data with expressions.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    age INT CHECK (age >= 18),\n    status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive')),\n    email TEXT CHECK (email LIKE '%@%'),\n    ...\n);\n\n-- Table-level CHECK\nCREATE TABLE products (\n    price FLOAT,\n    cost FLOAT,\n    CHECK (price >= cost)\n);\n```\n\n**Supported operators:**\n- Comparison: `=`, `!=`, `<>`, `<`, `>`, `<=`, `>=`\n- Range: `BETWEEN ... AND ...`\n- Set: `IN (...)`\n- Pattern: `LIKE` (with `%` and `_`)\n- Null: `IS NULL`, `IS NOT NULL`\n\n### FOREIGN KEY (v3.2.0+)\n\nMaintain referential integrity.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    user_id INT REFERENCES users(id),\n    ...\n);\n\n-- With ON DELETE/UPDATE actions\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    user_id INT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,\n    ...\n);\n```\n\n**Actions:**\n- `CASCADE`: Propagate changes\n- `SET NULL`: Set to NULL\n- `RESTRICT`: Prevent changes\n- `NO ACTION`: Same as RESTRICT\n\n### DEFAULT\n\nSet default value.\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n    status TEXT DEFAULT 'active',\n    ...\n);\n```\n\n## Operators\n\n### Comparison Operators\n\n| Operator | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `=` | Equal | `age = 25` |\n| `!=`, `<>` | Not equal | `status != 'inactive'` |\n| `<` | Less than | `age < 18` |\n| `>` | Greater than | `age > 65` |\n| `<=` | Less than or equal | `age <= 100` |\n| `>=` | Greater than or equal | `age >= 0` |\n| `IS NULL` | Is null | `email IS NULL` |\n| `IS NOT NULL` | Is not null | `email IS NOT NULL` |\n| `BETWEEN` | In range | `age BETWEEN 18 AND 65` |\n| `IN` | In set | `status IN ('active', 'pending')` |\n| `LIKE` | Pattern match | `name LIKE 'A%'` |\n\n### Logical Operators\n\n| Operator | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `AND` | Both conditions | `age > 18 AND status = 'active'` |\n| `OR` | Either condition | `status = 'active' OR status = 'pending'` |\n| `NOT` | Negation | `NOT status = 'inactive'` |\n\n### JSON Operators (v3.2.0+)\n\n| Operator | Description | Example |\n|----------|-------------|---------|\n| `->` | Extract JSON value | `metadata->city` |\n| `->>` | Extract as text | `metadata->>city` |\n\n## Backup Commands\n\n### BACKUP\n\nCreate database backup.\n\n```sql\nBACKUP DATABASE database_name TO '/path/to/backup';\nBACKUP DATABASE database_name TO '/path/to/backup' WITH ENCRYPTION 'password';\nBACKUP DATABASE database_name TO '/path/to/backup' WITH COMPRESSION gzip;\nBACKUP DATABASE database_name TO '/path/to/backup' \n    WITH ENCRYPTION 'password' COMPRESSION lz4 LEVEL 9;\n```\n\n### RESTORE\n\nRestore from backup.\n\n```sql\nRESTORE DATABASE database_name FROM '/path/to/backup';\nRESTORE DATABASE database_name FROM '/path/to/backup' WITH ENCRYPTION 'password';\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n### Complex Query Examples\n\n**Join with subquery:**\n```sql\nSELECT u.name, o.total\nFROM users u\nJOIN (\n    SELECT user_id, SUM(total) as total\n    FROM orders\n    WHERE created_at > '2024-01-01'\n    GROUP BY user_id\n) o ON u.id = o.user_id\nWHERE o.total > 1000;\n```\n\n**Correlated subquery with EXISTS:**\n```sql\nSELECT name FROM users u\nWHERE EXISTS (\n    SELECT 1 FROM orders o\n    WHERE o.user_id = u.id\n    AND o.total > (SELECT AVG(total) FROM orders)\n);\n```\n\n**JSON filtering:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM events\nWHERE metadata->type = 'purchase'\nAND (metadata->amount)::FLOAT > 100;\n```\n\n**Full-text search with ranking:**\n```sql\nSELECT title, MATCH(content) AGAINST('database') as relevance\nFROM articles\nWHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database')\nORDER BY relevance DESC\nLIMIT 10;\n```\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 42, "timestamp": 1783744323.5600312, "date": "2026-07-11", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 126757, Create base table\n    db.create_table(\"orders\", [\n        {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n        {'name': 'user_id', 'type': 'INT'},\n        {'name': 'total', 'type': 'FLOAT'},\n        {'name': 'status', 'type': 'TEXT'}\n    ])\n    \n    # Insert data\n    db.insert(\"orders\", [1, 1, 100.00, \"completed\"])\n    db.insert(\"orders\", [2, 1, 200.00, \"pending\"])\n    db.insert(\"orders\", [3, 2, 50.00, \"completed\"])\n    \n    print(\"Created orders table with 3 rows\")\n    \n    # Note: Views require view_manager, show concept\n    print(\"\\nView creation (conceptual):\")\n    print(\"  CREATE VIEW completed_orders AS\")\n    print(\"    SELECT * FROM orders WHERE status = 'completed'\")\n    print(\"  Would create virtual table for completed orders only\")\n\n\ndef demo_subqueries(db):\n    \"\"\"Demonstrate subqueries.\"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*60)\n    print(\"SUBQUERIES DEMO\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    \n    # Create tables\n    db.create_table(\"students\", [\n        {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n        {'name': 'name', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n        {'name': 'score', 'type': 'INT'}\n    ])\n    \n    db.create_table(\"grades\", [\n        {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n        {'name': 'student_id', 'type': 'INT'},\n        {'name': 'subject', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n        {'name': 'grade', 'type': 'INT'}\n    ])\n    \n    # Insert data\n    db.insert(\"students\", [1, \"Alice\", 85])\n    db.insert(\"students\", [2, \"Bob\", 75])\n    db.insert(\"students\", [3, \"Charlie\", 90])\n    \n    db.insert(\"grades\", [1, 1, \"Math\", 90])\n    db.insert(\"grades\", [2, 1, \"Science\", 85])\n    db.insert(\"grades\", [3, 2, \"Math\", 70])\n    \n    print(\"Created students and grades tables\")\n    \n    # Show subquery examples\n    print(\"\\nSubquery Examples:\")\n    print(\"1. Scalar subquery in SELECT:\")\n    print(\"   SELECT name, (SELECT AVG(score) FROM students) as avg_score\")\n    print(\"   FROM students\")\n    \n    print(\"\\n2. IN subquery:\")\n    print(\"   SELECT * FROM students\")\n    print(\"   WHERE id IN (SELECT student_id FROM grades WHERE grade > 80)\")\n    \n    print(\"\\n3. EXISTS subquery:\")\n    print(\"   SELECT * FROM students s\")\n    print(\"   WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM grades g WHERE g.student_id = s.id)\")\n    \n    print(\"\\n4. Correlated subquery:\")\n    print(\"   SELECT name,\")\n    print(\"     (SELECT AVG(grade) FROM grades WHERE student_id = students.id) as avg_grade\")\n    print(\"   FROM students\")\n\n\ndef demo_json(db):\n    \"\"\"Demonstrate JSON support.\"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*60)\n    print(\"JSON SUPPORT DEMO\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    \n    # Create table with JSON column\n    result = db.create_table(\"events\", [\n        {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n        {'name': 'type', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n        {'name': 'data', 'type': 'JSON'}\n    ])\n    print(f\"Create table with JSON: {result}\")\n    \n    # Insert JSON data\n    print(\"\\nInsert JSON data:\")\n    result = db.insert(\"events\", [1, \"click\", '{\"x\": 100, \"y\": 200, \"target\": \"button\"}'])\n    print(f\"  Click event: {result}\")\n    result = db.insert(\"events\", [2, \"purchase\", '{\"amount\": 99.99, \"currency\": \"USD\", \"items\": 3}'])\n    print(f\"  Purchase event: {result}\")\n    \n    # Query JSON\n    print(\"\\nQuery JSON data:\")\n    result = db.select(\"events\", [\"id\", \"type\"], raw=True)\n    for row in result:\n        print(f\"  Event {row['id']}: {row['type']}\")\n    \n    print(\"\\nJSON extraction examples:\")\n    print(\"  SELECT data->x FROM events WHERE type = 'click'\")\n    print(\"  SELECT data->>amount FROM events WHERE type = 'purchase'\")\n    print(\"  SELECT * FROM events WHERE data->>currency = 'USD'\")\n\n\ndef demo_query_optimization(db):\n    \"\"\"Demonstrate query optimization features.\"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*60)\n    print(\"QUERY OPTIMIZATION DEMO\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    \n    try:\n        from query_optimizer import QueryOptimizer\n        \n        optimizer = QueryOptimizer(cache_size=50)\n        print(\"Created query optimizer with cache size 50\")\n        \n        # Example queries\n        queries = [\n            \"SELECT * FROM products WHERE price > 100\",\n            \"SELECT * FROM employees WHERE dept_id = 1\",\n            \"SELECT * FROM products WHERE price > 100\",  # Repeat\n        ]\n        \n        print(\"\\nOptimizing queries:\")\n        for i, query in enumerate(queries, 1):\n            print(f\"\\n  Query {i}: {query}\")\n            plan = optimizer.optimize(query, use_cache=True)\n            print(f\"    Plan cost: {plan.total_cost}\")\n            print(f\"    Estimated rows: {plan.estimated_rows}\")\n        \n        # Show cache stats\n        print(\"\\nCache statistics:\")\n        stats = optimizer.get_cache_stats()\n        print(f\"  Size: {stats['size']} / {stats['max_size']}\")\n        print(f\"  Hit rate: {stats['hit_rate']:.2%}\")\n        print(f\"  Miss rate: {stats['miss_rate']:.2%}\")\n        \n        # Explain cache\n        print(\"\\n\" + optimizer.explain_cache())\n        \n    except ImportError:\n        print(\"Query optimizer not available\")\n\n\ndef demo_metrics():\n    \"\"\"Demonstrate metrics collection.\"\"\"\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*60)\n    print(\"METRICS DEMO\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    \n    try:\n        from metrics import KosDBMetrics\n        \n        metrics = KosDBMetrics()\n        print(\"Created metrics collector\")\n        \n        # Record some metrics\n        print(\"\\nRecording metrics:\")\n        \n        metrics.record_query(\"SELECT\", 0.05, success=True)\n        print(\"  Recorded SELECT query (0.05s)\")\n        \n        metrics.record_query(\"INSERT\", 0.02, success=True)\n        print(\"  Recorded INSERT query (0.02s)\")\n        \n        metrics.record_cache_hit(\"plan\")\n        print(\"  Recorded plan cache hit\")\n        \n        metrics.record_cache_miss(\"plan\")\n        print(\"  Recorded plan cache miss\")\n        \n        metrics.record_connection_opened()\n        print(\"  Recorded connection opened\")\n        \n        # Show Prometheus format\n        print(\"\\nPrometheus metrics output:\")\n        print(\"-\" * 40)\n        output = metrics.get_prometheus_metrics()\n        # Print first few lines\n        for line in output.split('\\n')[:15]:\n            print(line)\n        print(\"...\")\n        \n    except ImportError:\n        print(\"Metrics module not available\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Run all demonstrations.\"\"\"\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    print(\"KOSDB v3.2.0 FEATURES DEMONSTRATION\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    \n    # <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<CreateFile>\n<fileName>examples/sql_examples.sql</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>-- KosDB v3.2.0 SQL Examples\n-- Comprehensive examples of all new features\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 1. DATABASE SETUP\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create database\nCREATE DATABASE ecommerce;\nUSE ecommerce;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 2. CHECK CONSTRAINTS\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create table with CHECK constraints\nCREATE TABLE products (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    price FLOAT CHECK (price > 0),\n    quantity INT CHECK (quantity >= 0),\n    status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'discontinued')),\n    discount FLOAT CHECK (discount >= 0 AND discount <= 100),\n    \n    -- Table-level CHECK constraint\n    CHECK (price * (1 - discount/100) >= 0)\n);\n\n-- Valid inserts\nINSERT INTO products VALUES (1, 'Laptop', 999.99, 50, 'active', 10);\nINSERT INTO products VALUES (2, 'Mouse', 29.99, 100, 'active', 0);\nINSERT INTO products VALUES (3, 'Monitor', 299.99, 25, 'active', 15);\n\n-- Invalid inserts (will fail)\n-- INSERT INTO products VALUES (4, 'Invalid', -10, 10, 'active', 0);  -- Negative price\n-- INSERT INTO products VALUES (5, 'Invalid', 100, -5, 'active', 0);   -- Negative quantity\n-- INSERT INTO products VALUES (6, 'Invalid', 100, 10, 'unknown', 0); -- Invalid status\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 3. FOREIGN KEYS\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create parent table\nCREATE TABLE categories (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    description TEXT\n);\n\n-- Create child table with foreign key\nCREATE TABLE products_fk (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    category_id INT REFERENCES categories(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,\n    price FLOAT CHECK (price > 0)\n);\n\n-- Insert parent data first\nINSERT INTO categories VALUES (1, 'Electronics', 'Electronic devices');\nINSERT INTO categories VALUES (2, 'Books', 'Physical and digital books');\n\n-- Insert child data\nINSERT INTO products_fk VALUES (1, 'Laptop', 1, 999.99);\nINSERT INTO products_fk VALUES (2, 'Programming Book', 2, 49.99);\n\n-- This will fail (category 999 doesn't exist)\n-- INSERT INTO products_fk VALUES (3, 'Invalid', 999, 100);\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 4. ALTER TABLE OPERATIONS\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create base table\nCREATE TABLE customers (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL\n);\n\nINSERT INTO customers VALUES (1, 'Alice');\nINSERT INTO customers VALUES (2, 'Bob');\n\n-- ADD COLUMN\nALTER TABLE customers ADD COLUMN email TEXT;\nALTER TABLE customers ADD COLUMN phone TEXT;\nALTER TABLE customers ADD COLUMN status TEXT DEFAULT 'active';\n\n-- Verify columns added\nSELECT * FROM customers;\n\n-- RENAME COLUMN\nALTER TABLE customers RENAME COLUMN name TO full_name;\n\n-- MODIFY COLUMN type\nALTER TABLE customers MODIFY COLUMN phone VARCHAR(20);\n\n-- ADD INDEX\nALTER TABLE customers ADD INDEX idx_email (email);\nALTER TABLE customers ADD INDEX idx_status (status);\n\n-- ADD CONSTRAINT\nALTER TABLE customers ADD CONSTRAINT chk_email CHECK (email LIKE '%@%');\n\n-- DROP COLUMN (with CASCADE to remove dependent objects)\nALTER TABLE customers DROP COLUMN phone CASCADE;\n\n-- DROP INDEX\nALTER TABLE customers DROP INDEX idx_email;\n\n-- DROP CONSTRAINT\nALTER TABLE customers DROP CONSTRAINT chk_email;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 5. VIEWS\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create orders table\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    customer_id INT NOT NULL,\n    total FLOAT CHECK (total > 0),\n    status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'shipped', 'delivered')),\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (1, 1, 150.00, 'delivered', '2024-01-10');\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (2, 1, 75.50, 'shipped', '2024-01-12');\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (3, 2, 200.00, 'pending', '2024-01-15');\n\n-- Create view for completed orders\nCREATE VIEW completed_orders AS\nSELECT * FROM orders WHERE status = 'delivered';\n\n-- Query the view\nSELECT * FROM completed_orders;\n\n-- Create view with join\nCREATE VIEW customer_orders AS\nSELECT \n    c.full_name,\n    o.id as order_id,\n    o.total,\n    o.status\nFROM customers c\nJOIN orders o ON c.id = o.customer_id;\n\n-- Query the view\nSELECT * FROM customer_orders;\n\n-- Show all views\nSHOW VIEWS;\n\n-- Drop view\nDROP VIEW completed_orders;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 6. SUBQUERIES\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Scalar subquery in SELECT\nSELECT \n    full_name,\n    (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders WHERE customer_id = customers.id) as order_count\nFROM customers;\n\n-- Scalar subquery in WHERE\nSELECT * FROM products\nWHERE price > (SELECT AVG(price) FROM products);\n\n-- IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM customers\nWHERE id IN (SELECT customer_id FROM orders WHERE total > 100);\n\n-- NOT IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM customers\nWHERE id NOT IN (SELECT customer_id FROM orders);\n\n-- EXISTS subquery\nSELECT * FROM customers c\nWHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders o WHERE o.customer_id = c.id);\n\n-- NOT EXISTS subquery\nSELECT * FROM customers c\nWHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders o WHERE o.customer_id = c.id);\n\n-- Correlated subquery\nSELECT \n    full_name,\n    (SELECT MAX(total) FROM orders WHERE customer_id = customers.id) as max_order\nFROM customers;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 7. JSON SUPPORT\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create table with JSON column\nCREATE TABLE events (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    event_type TEXT,\n    event_data JSON,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Insert JSON data\nINSERT INTO events VALUES (1, 'click', '{\"x\": 100, \"y\": 200, \"target\": \"buy_button\"}');\nINSERT INTO events VALUES (2, 'purchase', '{\"amount\": 99.99, \"currency\": \"USD\", \"items\": [{\"id\": 1, \"qty\": 2}]}');\nINSERT INTO events VALUES (3, 'page_view', '{\"url\": \"/products\", \"referrer\": \"google\"}');\n\n-- Query with JSON extraction\nSELECT id, event_type, event_data->target FROM events WHERE event_type = 'click';\nSELECT id, event_type, event_data->>amount FROM events WHERE event_type = 'purchase';\n\n-- Filter by JSON value\nSELECT * FROM events WHERE event_data->>currency = 'USD';\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 8. FULL-TEXT SEARCH\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create articles table\nCREATE TABLE articles (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    title TEXT,\n    content TEXT,\n    author TEXT\n);\n\n-- Insert sample data\nINSERT INTO articles VALUES \n    (1, 'Introduction to Databases', 'Databases are essential for...', 'Alice'),\n    (2, 'SQL Optimization Tips', 'Optimizing SQL queries requires...', 'Bob'),\n    (3, 'Database Security', 'Securing your database is...', 'Alice');\n\n-- Create full-text index\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles(content);\n\n-- Natural language search\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database');\n\n-- Boolean mode search\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('+SQL -security' IN BOOLEAN MODE);\n\n-- With query expansion\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('optimization' WITH QUERY EXPANSION);\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 9. TRANSACTIONS\n-- ============================================\n\nBEGIN;\n\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (4, 1, 50.00, 'pending', CURRENT_TIMESTAMP);\nINSERT INTO orders VALUES (5, 2, 150.00, 'pending', CURRENT_TIMESTAMP);\n\n-- Commit or rollback\nCOMMIT;\n-- Or: ROLLBACK;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 10. QUERY OPTIMIZATION\n-- ============================================\n\n-- EXPLAIN query plan\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM products WHERE price > 100;\n\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM customers \nWHERE id IN (SELECT customer_id FROM orders WHERE total > 100);\n\n-- Show plan cache statistics\nEXPLAIN CACHE;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 11. BACKUP AND RESTORE\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create backup\nBACKUP DATABASE ecommerce TO '/backups/ecommerce.backup';\n\n-- Create encrypted backup\nBACKUP DATABASE ecommerce TO '/backups/ecommerce.backup' \nWITH ENCRYPTION 'my-secret-key';\n\n-- Restore from backup\nRESTORE DATABASE ecommerce FROM '/backups/ecommerce.backup';\n\n-- Restore with encryption\nRESTORE DATABASE ecommerce FROM '/backups/ecommerce.backup' \nWITH ENCRYPTION 'my-secret-key';\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 12. USER MANAGEMENT\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Create users\nCREATE USER admin PASSWORD 'admin123';\nCREATE USER analyst PASSWORD 'analyst123';\n\n-- Grant privileges\nGRANT ALL ON ecommerce.* TO admin;\nGRANT SELECT ON ecommerce.* TO analyst;\nGRANT INSERT, UPDATE ON ecommerce.orders TO analyst;\n\n-- Show grants\nSHOW GRANTS FOR admin;\nSHOW GRANTS FOR analyst;\n\n-- Revoke privileges\nREVOKE INSERT ON ecommerce.orders FROM analyst;\n\n-- Create role\nCREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only database access';\nGRANT SELECT ON ecommerce.* TO readonly;\nGRANT ROLE readonly TO analyst;\n\n-- Show roles\nSHOW ROLES;\n\n-- ============================================\n-- 13. CLEANUP\n-- ============================================\n\n-- Drop objects\nDROP VIEW IF EXISTS customer_orders;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS events;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS orders;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS customers;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS products;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS products_fk;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS categories;\nDROP TABLE IF EXISTS articles;\n\n-- Drop database\n-- DROP DATABASE ecommerce;\n</contentOfFile>\n</CreateFile>", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 42, "timestamp": 1783744370.2146475, "date": "2026-07-11", "thinking": "", "prompt_tokens": 134302, "response_tokens": 2150} -->

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# LevelDB Socket Server - Client Examples\n\nThis directory contains official client libraries and usage examples for connecting to the LevelDB Socket Server from PHP and Python applications.\n\n## Directory Structure\n\n```\nexamples/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 README.md              # This file\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 php/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 LevelDBClient.php  # PHP client library\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 basic_example.php  # Basic CRUD operations\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 replication_example.php  # Replication features\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 python/\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 leveldb_client.py  # Python client library\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 basic_example.py   # Basic CRUD operations\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 replication_example.py   # Replication features\n```\n\n## PHP Examples\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- PHP 7.4+ with sockets extension enabled\n- LevelDB server running (see main README)\n\n### Files\n\n- **LevelDBClient.php** - Full-featured client library with:\n  - Connection management\n  - Authentication\n  - CRUD operations\n  - Result parsing\n  - Replication support\n\n### Usage\n\n```php\n<?php\nrequire_once 'LevelDBClient.php';\n\n// Simple usage\n$client = new LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999);\n$client->connect();\n$client->authenticate('admin', 'admin');\n\n// Create database and table\n$client->createDatabase('myapp');\n$client->useDatabase('myapp');\n$client->createTable('users', ['id INT PRIMARY KEY', 'name TEXT']);\n\n// Insert data\n$client->insert('users', [1, 'John Doe']);\n\n// Query data\n$users = $client->select('users');\nforeach ($users as $user) {\n    echo $user['name'];\n}\n\n$client->close();\n?>\n```\n\n### Run Examples\n\n```bash\ncd examples/php\nphp basic_example.php\nphp replication_example.php\n```\n\n## Python Examples\n\n### Prerequisites\n\n- Python 3.7+\n- LevelDB server running (see main README)\n\n### Files\n\n- **leveldb_client.py** - Full-featured client library with:\n  - Synchronous and async support\n  - Context managers for easy resource management\n  - Type hints for better IDE support\n  - Result parsing\n  - Connection pooling ready\n\n### Usage\n\n```python\nfrom leveldb_client import LevelDBClient, connect\n\n# Method 1: Context manager (recommended)\nwith connect('localhost', 9999, 'admin', 'admin') as db:\n    db.create_database('myapp')\n    db.use('myapp')\n    db.create_table('users', ['id INT', 'name TEXT'])\n    db.insert('users', [1, 'John'])\n    result = db.select('users')\n    print(result)\n\n# Method 2: Direct usage\nclient = LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999)\nclient.connect()\nclient.auth('admin', 'admin')\nresult = client.query(\"SELECT * FROM users\")\nclient.close()\n```\n\n### Run Examples\n\n```bash\ncd examples/python\npython basic_example.py\npython replication_example.py\n```\n\n## Quick Reference\n\n### Connection\n\n| Language | Code |\n|----------|------|\n| PHP | `$client = new LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999);` |\n| Python | `client = LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999)` |\n\n### Authentication\n\n| Language | Code |\n|----------|------|\n| PHP | `$client->authenticate('admin', 'admin');` |\n| Python | `client.auth('admin', 'admin')` |\n\n### Create Database\n\n| Language | Code |\n|----------|------|\n| PHP | `$client->createDatabase('mydb');` |\n| Python | `client.create_database('mydb')` |\n\n### Insert\n\n| Language | Code |\n|----------|------|\n| PHP | `$client->insert('users', [1, 'John']);` |\n| Python | `client.insert('users', [1, 'John'])` |\n\n### Select\n\n| Language | Code |\n|----------|------|\n| PHP | `$users = $client->select('users', 'age>18');` |\n| Python | `users = client.select('users', 'age>18')` |\n\n## Advanced Features\n\n### PHP Advanced\n\n```php\n// Replication status\n$status = $client->showMasterStatus();\n$status = $client->showSlaveStatus();\n\n// List databases/tables\n$databases = $client->listDatabases();\n$tables = $client->listTables();\n\n// Raw query\n$result = $client->execute(\"SELECT * FROM users WHERE id=1\");\n```\n\n### Python Advanced\n\n```python\n# Async client for high performance\nfrom leveldb_client import AsyncLevelDBClient\nimport asyncio\n\nasync def main():\n    async with AsyncLevelDBClient() as db:\n        await db.auth('admin', 'admin')\n        result = await db.execute(\"SELECT * FROM users\")\n\nasyncio.run(main())\n\n# Context manager\nfrom leveldb_client import connect\n\nwith connect('localhost', 9999, 'admin', 'admin') as db:\n    result = db.select('users')\n```\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### PHP\n\n```php\ntry {\n    $client = new LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999);\n    $client->connect();\n    $client->authenticate('admin', 'wrongpass');\n} catch (Exception $e) {\n    echo \"Error: \" . $e->getMessage();\n}\n```\n\n### Python\n\n```python\nfrom leveldb_client import LevelDBClient, AuthenticationError\n\ntry:\n    client = LevelDBClient('localhost', 9999)\n    client.connect()\n    client.auth('admin', 'wrongpass')\nexcept AuthenticationError as e:\n    print(f\"Auth failed: {e}\")\nexcept ConnectionError as e:\n    print(f\"Connection failed: {e}\")\n```\n\n## Best Practices\n\n1. **Always use context managers** (Python) or **try-finally** (PHP) to ensure connections close\n2. **Reuse connections** when making multiple queries\n3. **Handle exceptions** properly in production code\n4. **Use prepared statements** concept - validate inputs before sending\n5. **Set appropriate timeouts** based on your network latency\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Refused\n- Check if server is running: `python server.py`\n- Verify host and port are correct\n- Check firewall settings\n\n### Authentication Failed\n- Verify username and password\n- Check if user exists: `SHOW USERS` as admin\n- Create user if needed: `CREATE REPLICATION USER`\n\n### Timeout\n- Increase timeout in client constructor\n- Check network connectivity\n- Verify server is responsive\n\n## Contributing\n\nWhen adding new examples:\n1. Follow existing code style\n2. Include error handling\n3. Add comments explaining complex operations\n4. Update this README\n\n## License\n\nSame as main project (MIT)# LevelDB Socket Server - Client Examples\n\nThis directory contains official client libraries and usage examples for connecting to the
