# KosDB v3.2.0
> 
> A high-performance, feature-rich LevelDB-based database server with SQL-like interface, replication, TLS encryption, GPU acceleration, comprehensive audit logging, and advanced query capabilities.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> ### Core Database
> - **SQL-like Interface**: Familiar CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE commands
> - **Multiple Databases**: Support for multiple named databases
> - **Table Schema**: Define columns with types (INT, TEXT, FLOAT, JSON, etc.)
> - **Transactions**: ACID-complia...
> (truncated, 14130 chars total)

---

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# KosDB v3.2.0\n\nA high-performance, feature-rich LevelDB-based database server with SQL-like interface, replication, TLS encryption, GPU acceleration, comprehensive audit logging, and advanced query capabilities.\n\n## Features\n\n### Core Database\n- **SQL-like Interface**: Familiar CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE commands\n- **Multiple Databases**: Support for multiple named databases\n- **Table Schema**: Define columns with types (INT, TEXT, FLOAT, JSON, etc.)\n- **Transactions**: ACID-compliant operations with BEGIN, COMMIT, ROLLBACK\n- **Indexing**: Primary, secondary, and full-text index support\n- **Views**: Virtual tables based on SELECT queries\n- **Subqueries**: Scalar, IN/NOT IN, EXISTS/NOT EXISTS, correlated subqueries\n\n### Security (New in v3.1.0+)\n- **TLS/SSL Encryption**: Secure client-server communication\n  - Certificate-based authentication\n  - Self-signed certificate generation\n  - Client certificate verification (mTLS)\n- **At-Rest Encryption**: AES-256-GCM database encryption\n  - PBKDF2 key derivation\n  - Master key rotation support\n- **Audit Logging**: Comprehensive operation logging\n  - Multiple output targets (file, syslog, webhook)\n  - Log rotation and compression\n  - Sensitive command masking\n\n### Authentication & Authorization\n- **Database-backed Authentication**: Username/password with bcrypt hashing\n- **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)**: Create roles and assign to users\n- **Granular Permissions**: SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE, CREATE, DROP, ALTER, INDEX, REFERENCES, ADMIN\n- **Column-level Security**: Restrict access to specific columns\n- **Session Management**: JWT-based sessions with TTL\n\n### Replication & High Availability\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Automatic failover support\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multi-master with conflict resolution\n- **Async Replication**: Non-blocking replication\n- **Replication Lag Monitoring**: Track replication health\n\n### Query Optimization (New in v3.2.0)\n- **Query Plan Caching**: LRU cache for parsed execution plans\n- **Cost-Based Optimizer**: Statistics-driven plan selection\n- **Semi-Join Optimization**: Efficient IN/EXISTS subquery execution\n- **Index Advisor**: Automatic index recommendations\n- **Query Statistics**: Execution metrics and profiling\n\n### Advanced SQL (New in v3.2.0)\n- **CHECK Constraints**: Data validation with complex expressions\n- **Foreign Keys**: Referential integrity with CASCADE/SET NULL/RESTRICT\n- **ALTER TABLE**: Add/drop/modify columns, indexes, constraints\n- **JSON Support**: Native JSON columns with path extraction\n- **Full-Text Search**: MATCH ... AGAINST syntax with relevance scoring\n- **Subqueries**: Scalar, IN, EXISTS, correlated subqueries\n\n### Performance Features\n- **GPU Acceleration**: CUDA-powered query processing\n  - Vector operations\n  - Matrix multiplication\n  - Sorting algorithms\n- **Connection Pooling**: Efficient connection management\n- **Query Caching**: Result cache for frequent queries\n- **Plan Caching**: Execution plan cache for repeated queries\n- **Compression**: Multiple algorithms (gzip, lz4, zstd)\n\n### Monitoring (New in v3.2.0)\n- **Prometheus Metrics**: Query counts, latency, cache hit rates\n- **Health Checks**: Liveness and readiness endpoints\n- **Detailed Status**: Server status via HTTP API\n- **Cache Statistics**: Plan cache performance metrics\n\n### Backup & Recovery\n- **Hot Backups**: Non-blocking backup operations\n- **Encrypted Backups**: Password-protected backup files\n- **Compression Options**: gzip, lz4, zstd\n- **Point-in-Time Recovery**: Restore to specific timestamp\n- **Integrity Verification**: SHA-256 checksums\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Installation\n\n```bash\n# Clone repository\ngit clone https://github.com/yourusername/kosdb.git\ncd kosdb\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# Optional: Install GPU support\npip install pycuda  # For CUDA acceleration\n\n# Optional: Install encryption\npip install cryptography  # For TLS and at-rest encryption\n```\n\n### Basic Usage\n\n```bash\n# Start server with default config\npython server.py\n\n# Or specify configuration file\npython server.py -c config.json\n\n# Create admin user\npython server.py --prepare_admin admin --prepare_password secret123\n```\n\n### Client Connection\n\n```bash\n# Connect with CLI client\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 -u admin -P secret123\n\n# Or use with TLS\npython cli.py -H localhost -p 9999 --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Basic Configuration (config.json)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"version\": \"3.2.0\",\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9999,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\"\n  },\n  \"database\": {\n    \"engine\": \"leveldb\",\n    \"compression\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### TLS Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"/etc/kosdb/ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Metrics and Monitoring (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"collection_interval\": 15,\n    \"retention_days\": 30\n  }\n}\n```\n\nAccess metrics at:\n- `http://localhost:9090/metrics` - Prometheus format\n- `http://localhost:9090/health` - Health checks\n- `http://localhost:9090/status` - Detailed status\n\n### Query Optimizer Configuration (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"collect_statistics\": true,\n    \"enable_semi_join\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Audit Logging Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"audit_logging\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"log_dir\": \"./audit_logs\",\n    \"max_size_mb\": 100,\n    \"max_age_days\": 30,\n    \"targets\": [\"file\", \"syslog\"],\n    \"exclude_commands\": [\"PING\"],\n    \"mask_commands\": [\"PASS\", \"PASSWORD\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### GPU Configuration\n\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8,\n    \"kernels\": [\"vector_ops\", \"matrix_mult\", \"sort\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\nSee [Configuration Guide](README_CONFIG.md) for complete documentation.\n\n## SQL Commands\n\n### Database Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create database\nCREATE DATABASE mydb;\n\n-- Use database\nUSE mydb;\n\n-- Drop database\nDROP DATABASE mydb;\n```\n\n### Table Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Create table with constraints\nCREATE TABLE users (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    name TEXT NOT NULL,\n    email TEXT UNIQUE,\n    age INT CHECK (age >= 18),\n    metadata JSON,\n    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Create table with foreign key\nCREATE TABLE orders (\n    id INT PRIMARY KEY,\n    user_id INT REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n    total FLOAT CHECK (total > 0),\n    status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'shipped', 'delivered'))\n);\n\n-- Describe table\nDESCRIBE users;\n\n-- Drop table\nDROP TABLE users;\n```\n\n### ALTER TABLE (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Add column\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN phone TEXT;\n\n-- Add column with constraints\nALTER TABLE users ADD COLUMN status TEXT CHECK (status IN ('active', 'inactive'));\n\n-- Drop column\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN phone;\n\n-- Drop column with CASCADE\nALTER TABLE users DROP COLUMN email CASCADE;\n\n-- Modify column type\nALTER TABLE users MODIFY COLUMN age FLOAT;\n\n-- Rename column\nALTER TABLE users RENAME COLUMN name TO full_name;\n\n-- Add index\nALTER TABLE users ADD INDEX idx_email (email);\n\n-- Drop index\nALTER TABLE users DROP INDEX idx_email;\n\n-- Add foreign key constraint\nALTER TABLE orders ADD CONSTRAINT fk_user FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id);\n\n-- Add CHECK constraint\nALTER TABLE users ADD CONSTRAINT chk_age CHECK (age >= 18);\n\n-- Drop constraint\nALTER TABLE users DROP CONSTRAINT chk_age;\n```\n\n### Data Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Insert\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'Alice', 'alice@example.com', 30, '{\"city\": \"NYC\"}');\n\n-- Insert with JSON\nINSERT INTO users VALUES (2, 'Bob', 'bob@example.com', 25, '{\"city\": \"LA\", \"hobbies\": [\"reading\"]}');\n\n-- Select\nSELECT * FROM users;\nSELECT name, email FROM users WHERE age > 25;\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE name LIKE 'A%';\n\n-- JSON extraction\nSELECT name, metadata->city FROM users;\nSELECT name, metadata->>city FROM users;  -- As text\n\n-- Update\nUPDATE users SET age = 31 WHERE id = 1;\n\n-- Delete\nDELETE FROM users WHERE id = 1;\n```\n\n### Subqueries (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Scalar subquery\nSELECT name, (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders) as order_count FROM users;\n\n-- IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders WHERE total > 100);\n\n-- NOT IN subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE id NOT IN (SELECT user_id FROM orders);\n\n-- EXISTS subquery\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM orders WHERE orders.user_id = users.id);\n\n-- Correlated subquery\nSELECT name, (SELECT MAX(total) FROM orders WHERE orders.user_id = users.id) as max_order\nFROM users;\n```\n\n### Views (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Create view\nCREATE VIEW active_users AS\nSELECT * FROM users WHERE status = 'active';\n\n-- Query view\nSELECT * FROM active_users WHERE age > 25;\n\n-- Drop view\nDROP VIEW active_users;\n\n-- Show views\nSHOW VIEWS;\n```\n\n### Full-Text Search (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Create full-text index\nCREATE FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles(content);\n\n-- Search with natural language mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('database optimization');\n\n-- Search with boolean mode\nSELECT * FROM articles WHERE MATCH(content) AGAINST('+database -mysql' IN BOOLEAN MODE);\n\n-- Drop full-text index\nDROP FULLTEXT INDEX idx_content ON articles;\n```\n\n### User Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create user\nCREATE USER alice PASSWORD 'secret123';\n\n-- Grant privileges\nGRANT SELECT, INSERT ON mydb.users TO alice;\n\n-- Revoke privileges\nREVOKE DELETE ON mydb.users FROM alice;\n\n-- Show grants\nSHOW GRANTS FOR alice;\n```\n\n### Role Management\n\n```sql\n-- Create role\nCREATE ROLE readonly DESCRIPTION 'Read-only access';\n\n-- Grant privileges to role\nGRANT SELECT ON *.* TO readonly;\n\n-- Assign role to user\nGRANT ROLE readonly TO alice;\n\n-- Show roles\nSHOW ROLES;\n```\n\n### Transactions\n\n```sql\n-- Begin transaction\nBEGIN TRANSACTION;\n\n-- Or simply\nBEGIN;\n\n-- Commit\nCOMMIT;\n\n-- Rollback\nROLLBACK;\n```\n\n### Backup Operations\n\n```sql\n-- Backup with encryption\nBACKUP DATABASE mydb TO /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword' COMPRESSION gzip;\n\n-- Restore with encryption\nRESTORE DATABASE mydb FROM /backups/mydb.backup WITH ENCRYPTION 'mypassword';\n```\n\n### Query Optimization (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```sql\n-- Explain query plan\nEXPLAIN SELECT * FROM users WHERE age > 25;\n\n-- Show plan cache status\nEXPLAIN CACHE;\n\n-- Analyze table for statistics\nANALYZE TABLE users;\n```\n\n## Environment Variables\n\nSensitive configuration values can be stored in environment variables:\n\n```bash\n# Encryption passphrase\nexport KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE=\"my-secret-key\"\n\n# TLS certificate password\nexport KOSDB_TLS_PASSWORD=\"cert-password\"\n\n# Backup encryption\nexport KOSDB_BACKUP_PASSPHRASE=\"backup-secret\"\n\n# JWT secret\nexport KOSDB_JWT_SECRET=\"jwt-signing-key\"\n```\n\nReference in config.json:\n```json\n{\n  \"database\": {\n    \"encryption\": {\n      \"passphrase_env\": \"KOSDB_ENCRYPTION_PASSPHRASE\"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Security Hardening\n\n### TLS Setup\n\n1. Generate CA and server certificates:\n```bash\n# Generate CA\nopenssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout ca.key -out ca.crt -days 365 -nodes\n\n# Generate server certificate\nopenssl req -newkey rsa:4096 -keyout server.key -out server.csr -nodes\nopenssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 365\n```\n\n2. Configure server:\n```json\n{\n  \"tls\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"cert_file\": \"server.crt\",\n    \"key_file\": \"server.key\",\n    \"ca_file\": \"ca.crt\",\n    \"client_auth\": false\n  }\n}\n```\n\n3. Connect client with TLS:\n```bash\npython cli.py --tls --ca-cert ca.crt -u admin -P secret123\n```\n\n### Encryption Best Practices\n\n1. **Use strong passphrases** (minimum 16 characters)\n2. **Store keys securely** (use key files with restricted permissions)\n3. **Rotate keys regularly** (use `ROTATE KEY` command)\n4. **Backup keys separately** from encrypted data\n5. **Enable audit logging** for encryption operations\n\n## Performance Tuning\n\n### GPU Acceleration\n\nEnable GPU for large-scale operations:\n```json\n{\n  \"gpu\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"device_id\": 0,\n    \"memory_fraction\": 0.8\n  }\n}\n```\n\nGPU-accelerated operations:\n- Vector mathematical operations\n- Matrix multiplication\n- Large dataset sorting\n- Aggregate functions\n\n### Query Plan Caching (New in v3.2.0)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"optimizer\": {\n    \"cache_size\": 100,\n    \"invalidate_on_schema_change\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Connection Pooling\n\n```json\n{\n  \"performance\": {\n    \"connection_pool_min\": 5,\n    \"connection_pool_max\": 20,\n    \"query_cache_size\": 1000\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Health Check\n\n```bash\n# Check server health via HTTP\ncurl http://localhost:9090/health\n\n# Check via CLI\npython cli.py -c \"SHOW STATUS\"\n```\n\n### Metrics\n\nEnable Prometheus metrics:\n```json\n{\n  \"metrics\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 9090,\n    \"prometheus_enabled\": true\n  }\n}\n```\n\nAccess metrics:\n- `http://localhost:9090/metrics` - Prometheus format\n- `http://localhost:9090/health` - Health status\n- `http://localhost:9090/health/live` - Liveness probe\n- `http://localhost:9090/health/ready` - Readiness probe\n- `http://localhost:9090/status` - Detailed server status\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Issues\n\n- Verify server is running: `python cli.py -c \"PING\"`\n- Check firewall rules for port 9999\n- Verify TLS certificates are valid\n\n### Performance Issues\n\n- Check query cache hit rate: `EXPLAIN CACHE`\n- Monitor replication lag\n- Review slow query log\n- Check plan cache statistics\n\n### Encryption Issues\n\n- Verify passphrase is correct\n- Check key file permissions (should be 600)\n- Ensure cryptography library is installed\n\n## Migration from v3.1 to v3.2\n\nSee [MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md](MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md) for detailed migration guide.\n\n## API Reference\n\nSee [API Documentation](docs/API.md) for detailed command reference.\n\n## Contributing\n\nSee [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md) for contribution guidelines.\n\n## License\n\nMIT License - <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# Changelog\n\nAll notable changes to KosDB will be documented in this file.\n\n## [3.2.0] - 2024-01-15\n\n### Added\n\n#### Query Optimization\n- **Query Plan Caching**: LRU cache for parsed execution plans with configurable size\n- **Cost-Based Optimizer**: Statistics-driven plan selection for better query performance\n- **Semi-Join Optimization**: Efficient IN/EXISTS subquery execution using semi-join transformation\n- **Index Advisor**: Automatic index recommendations based on query patterns\n- **Plan Cache Statistics**: Hit rate, miss rate, eviction tracking via EXPLAIN CACHE command\n\n#### Subquery Support\n- **Scalar Subqueries**: Support for (SELECT ...) in SELECT and WHERE clauses\n- **IN/NOT IN Subqueries**: Single column result subqueries with negation support\n- **EXISTS/NOT EXISTS Subqueries**: Correlated and non-correlated existence checks\n- **Correlated Subqueries**: Outer reference resolution for complex queries\n- **Semi-Join Transformation**: Query optimizer rewrites IN/EXISTS to semi-joins where applicable\n\n#### Advanced Constraints\n- **CHECK Constraints**: Data validation with complex expressions (=, !=, <, >, <=, >=, IN, BETWEEN, LIKE, IS NULL)\n- **Foreign Key Constraints**: Referential integrity with CASCADE, SET NULL, RESTRICT options\n- **Unique Constraints**: Multi-column unique constraints with automatic index creation\n\n#### ALTER TABLE Operations\n- **ADD COLUMN**: Add columns with full type support and constraints\n- **DROP COLUMN**: Remove columns with CASCADE handling for dependent objects\n- **MODIFY COLUMN**: Change column types with data validation\n- **RENAME COLUMN**: Rename existing columns with constraint updates\n- **ADD/DROP INDEX**: Dynamic index management\n- **ADD/DROP CONSTRAINT**: Foreign key, unique, and CHECK constraint management\n\n#### Views\n- **CREATE VIEW**: Virtual tables based on SELECT queries\n- **DROP VIEW**: View removal with dependency checking\n- **SHOW VIEWS**: List all views in database\n\n#### Full-Text Search\n- **MATCH ... AGAINST**: Natural language and boolean mode search\n- **Full-Text Indexes**: Inverted index for text search\n- **Relevance Scoring**: TF-IDF based result ranking\n- **Query Expansion**: Automatic synonym expansion\n\n#### JSON Support\n- **JSON Columns**: Native JSON data type storage\n- **JSON Extraction**: column->path and column->>path operators\n- **JSON Validation**: Automatic JSON format validation\n\n#### Monitoring and Metrics\n- **Prometheus Metrics**: Query counts, latency, cache hit rates, connection stats\n- **Health Endpoints**: /health, /health/live, /health/ready for container orchestration\n- **Status Endpoint**: /status for detailed server status\n- **Configurable Collection**: Metrics collection interval and retention settings\n\n#### SQL Enhancements\n- **EXPLAIN**: Query execution plan visualization\n- **EXPLAIN CACHE**: Plan cache status and statistics\n- **Transactions**: BEGIN, COMMIT, ROLLBACK support\n- **JSON Operators**: -> and ->> for JSON path extraction\n\n### Changed\n\n- **Parser**: Enhanced to support subqueries and complex WHERE clauses\n- **Query Optimizer**: Major rewrite with cost-based optimization\n- **Schema Storage**: Extended to support CHECK constraints and foreign keys\n- **Configuration**: New metrics and optimizer sections in config.json\n\n### Performance Improvements\n\n- Query plan caching reduces parsing overhead for repeated queries\n- Semi-join optimization improves IN/EXISTS subquery performance\n- Index recommendations help optimize query patterns\n- Connection metrics help identify bottlenecks\n\n### Deprecated\n\n- None\n\n### Removed\n\n- None\n\n### Security\n\n- Added privilege checks for ALTER TABLE operations\n- Constraint validation prevents data integrity violations\n- Foreign key enforcement maintains referential integrity\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- Fixed query parsing for complex nested conditions\n- Improved error messages for constraint violations\n- Fixed index updates during column modifications\n\n## [3.1.0] - 2023-12-01\n\n### Added\n\n#### Security Features\n- **TLS/SSL Encryption**: Certificate-based authentication and mTLS support\n- **At-Rest Encryption**: AES-256-GCM database encryption with PBKDF2\n- **Audit Logging**: Comprehensive operation logging with multiple targets\n- **Role-Based Access Control**: Granular permissions and role management\n\n#### Replication\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Automatic failover support\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Multi-master with conflict resolution\n- **Async Replication**: Non-blocking replication\n\n#### Performance\n- **GPU Acceleration**: CUDA-powered query processing\n- **Connection Pooling**: Efficient connection management\n- **Query Caching**: Result cache for frequent queries\n\n#### Backup & Recovery\n- **Hot Backups**: Non-blocking encrypted backups\n- **Compression**: Multiple algorithms (gzip, lz4, zstd)\n- **Point-in-Time Recovery**: Restore to specific timestamp\n\n## [3.0.0] - 2023-10-15\n\n### Added\n\n- Initial release of KosDB\n- SQL-like interface with basic CRUD operations\n- Multiple database support\n- Primary and secondary indexing\n- User authentication and basic authorization\n- Binary logging for replication\n\n### Features\n\n- CREATE, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE operations\n- Multiple databases with USE command\n- Table schema with column types\n- Primary key and index support\n- Basic user management\n\n## Migration Notes\n\n### Upgrading to 3.2.0 from 3.1.0\n\n1. **Configuration Updates**:\n   - Add `optimizer` section to config.json\n   - Add `metrics` section for monitoring\n   - Update version to \"3.2.0\"\n\n2. **Schema Compatibility**:\n   - Existing databases are fully compatible\n   - New CHECK constraints apply to future INSERT/UPDATE only\n   - Foreign keys can be added to existing tables via ALTER TABLE\n\n3. **API Changes**:\n   - New ALTER TABLE commands available\n   - Subqueries now supported in WHERE clauses\n   - EXPLAIN command added for query analysis\n\n4. **Monitoring Setup**:\n   - Configure metrics endpoint for Prometheus\n   - Set up health checks for container orchestration\n\nSee [MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md](MIGRATION_v3.1_to_v3.2.md) for detailed instructions.\n\n## Future Roadmap\n\n### Planned for 3.3.0\n- Window functions (ROW_NUMBER, RANK, etc.)\n- Common Table Expressions (CTEs)\n- Prepared statements\n- Stored procedures\n\n### Planned for 4.0.0\n- Distributed transactions\n- Sharding support\n- Columnar storage option\n- Vector search capabilities\n", "sessionId": 327, "rowId": 43, "timestamp": 1783744414.309531, "date": "2026-07-11", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

Run tests\n        runner = unittest.TextTestRunner(verbosity=2)\n        result = runner.run(suite)\n        \n        # Return summary\n        return {\n            'name': module_name,\n            'run': result.testsRun,\n            'failures': len(result.failures),\n            'errors': len(result.errors),\n            'skipped': len(result.skipped),\n            'success': result.wasSuccessful()\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"ERROR loading {module_name}: {e}\")\n        traceback.print_exc()\n        return {\n            'name': module_name,\n            'run': 0,\n            'failures': 0,\n            'errors': 1,\n            'skipped': 0,\n            'success': False,\n            'error_msg': str(e)\n        }\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Run all tests and report results.\"\"\"\n    print(\"=\"*70)\n    print(\"KOSDB v3.2.0 COMPREHENSIVE TEST SUITE\")\n    print(\"=\"*70)\n    \n    results = []\n    total_run = 0\n    total_failures = 0\n    total_errors = 0\n    total_skipped = 0\n    \n    for module_name in TEST_MODULES:\n        result = run_test_module(module_name)\n        results.append(result)\n        \n        total_run += result['run']\n        total_failures += result['failures']\n        total_errors += result['errors']\n        total_skipped += result['skipped']\n    \n    # <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nTest CHECK Constraints for KosDB v3.2.0\n\nTests:\n- CHECK with comparison operators (=, !=, <, >, <=, >=)\n- CHECK with IN operator\n- CHECK with BETWEEN operator\n- CHECK with LIKE operator\n- CHECK with IS NULL / IS NOT NULL\n- Multiple CHECK constraints\n- CHECK constraint validation on INSERT\n- CHECK constraint validation on UPDATE\n- Error messages for constraint violations\n\"\"\"\n\nimport unittest\nimport sys\nimport os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\n\n# Add parent directory to path\nsys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))\n\nfrom database import Database\nfrom parser import CommandParser\n\n\nclass TestCheckConstraints(unittest.TestCase):\n    \"\"\"Test CHECK constraint functionality.\"\"\"\n    \n    def setUp(self):\n        \"\"\"Set up test database.\"\"\"\n        self.temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()\n        self.db = Database(self.temp_dir, server_id=1)\n        self.parser = CommandParser()\n        \n        # Create test database\n        self.db.create_database(\"testdb\")\n        self.db.use_database(\"testdb\")\n    \n    def tearDown(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up test database.\"\"\"\n        self.db.close()\n        shutil.rmtree(self.temp_dir)\n    \n    def test_check_greater_than(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with > operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"products\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'price', 'type': 'FLOAT'},\n            {'name': 'quantity', 'type': 'INT', 'check': {'expression': 'quantity > 0'}}\n        ])\n        \n        # Valid insert\n        result = self.db.insert(\"products\", [1, 10.99, 5])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        # Invalid insert\n        result = self.db.insert(\"products\", [2, 5.99, 0])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n        self.assertIn(\"CHECK constraint violation\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_less_than_or_equal(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with <= operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"students\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'name', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n            {'name': 'grade', 'type': 'INT', 'check': {'expression': 'grade <= [2, \"Bob\", 105])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_equal(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with = operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"status_table\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'status', 'type': 'INT', 'check': {'expression': 'status = 1'}}\n        ])\n        \n        result =  \n    def test_check_not_equal(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with != operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"users\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'name', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n            {'name': 'age', 'type': 'INT', 'check': {'expression': 'age != 0'}}\n        ])\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"users\", [1, \"Alice\", 25])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"users\", [2, \"Bob\", 0])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_in_operator(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with IN operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"orders\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'status', 'type': 'TEXT', 'check': {'expression': \"status IN ('pending', 'shipped', 'delivered')\"}}\n        ])\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"orders\", [1, \"pending\"])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"orders\", [2, \"cancelled\"])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n        self.assertIn(\"not in\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_between_operator(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with BETWEEN operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"scores\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'player', 'type': 'TEXT'},\n            {'name': 'score', 'type': 'INT', 'check': {'expression': 'score BETWEEN 0 AND 100'}}\n        ])\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"scores\", [1, \"Alice\", 75])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"scores\", [2, \"Bob\", 150])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n        self.assertIn(\"not between\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_like_operator(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with LIKE operator.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"codes\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'code', 'type': 'TEXT', 'check': {'expression': \"code LIKE 'PRD-%'\"}}\n        ])\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"codes\", [1, \"PRD-001\"])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"codes\", [2, \"INVALID\"])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n        self.assertIn(\"not LIKE\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_is_null(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with IS NULL.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"optional\", [\n            {'name': 'id', 'type': 'INT', 'primary_key': True},\n            {'name': 'data', 'type': 'TEXT', 'check': {'expression': 'data IS NULL'}}\n        ])\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"optional\", [1, None])\n        self.assertIn(\"Inserted\", result)\n        \n        result = self.db.insert(\"optional\", [2, \"value\"])\n        self.assertIn(\"ERROR\", result)\n    \n    def test_check_is_not_null(self):\n        \"\"\"Test CHECK with IS NOT NULL.\"\"\"\n        self.db.create_table(\"required\", [\n            {'name': <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nTest Query Plan Cache for KosDB v3.2.0\n\nTests:\n- Plan cache storage and retrieval\n- LRU eviction policy\n- Cache invalidation on schema changes\n- Cache statistics (hit rate, miss rate, evictions)\n- EXPLAIN CACHE command\n- Cache dependency tracking\n\"\"\"\n\nimport unittest\nimport sys\nimport os\nimport tempfile\nimport shutil\nimport time\n\n# Add parent directory to path\nsys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))\n\nfrom query_optimizer import (\n    QueryOptimizer, PlanCache, ExecutionPlan, Operator, OperatorType,\n    Statistics, CostModel\n)\n\n\nclass TestPlanCache(unittest.TestCase):\n    \"\"\"Test plan cache functionality.\"\"\"\n    \n    def setUp(self):\n        \"\"\"Set up test cache.\"\"\"\n        self.cache = PlanCache(max_size=5)\n    \n    def test_cache_put_and_get(self):\n        \"\"\"Test basic cache put and get.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        # Put plan in cache\n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        \n        # Get plan from cache\n        retrieved = self.cache.get(\"key1\")\n        \n        self.assertIsNotNone(retrieved)\n        self.assertEqual(retrieved.total_cost, plan.total_cost)\n    \n    def test_cache_miss(self):\n        \"\"\"Test cache miss returns None.\"\"\"\n        result = self.cache.get(\"nonexistent\")\n        self.assertIsNone(result)\n        self.assertEqual(self.cache.stats['misses'], 1)\n    \n    def test_cache_hit_updates_stats(self):\n        \"\"\"Test cache hit updates statistics.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        \n        # First access\n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")\n        self.assertEqual(self.cache.stats['hits'], 1)\n        \n        # Second access\n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")\n        self.assertEqual(self.cache.stats['hits'], 2)\n    \n    def test_lru_eviction(self):\n        \"\"\"Test LRU eviction when cache is full.\"\"\"\n        # Fill cache to capacity\n        for i in range(5):\n            plan = self._create_dummy_plan(cost=i)\n            self.cache.put(f\"key{i}\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        \n        # All 5 should be in cache\n        self.assertEqual(len(self.cache.cache), 5)\n        \n        # Access key0 to make it recently used\n        self.cache.get(\"key0\")\n        \n        # Add 6th entry - should evict key1 (least recently used)\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan(cost=99)\n        self.cache.put(\"key5\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        \n        self.assertEqual(len(self.cache.cache), 5)\n        self.assertIn(\"key0\", self.cache.cache)  # Recently accessed\n        self.assertIn(\"key5\", self.cache.cache)  # Just added\n        self.assertNotIn(\"key1\", self.cache.cache)  # Evicted\n    \n    def test_cache_invalidation_by_table(self):\n        \"\"\"Test invalidating cache entries by table.\"\"\"\n        # Add plans depending on different tables\n        plan1 = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        plan2 = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan1, {\"users\"})\n        self.cache.put(\"key2\", plan2, {\"orders\"})\n        \n        # Invalidate by table\n        self.cache.invalidate(\"users\")\n        \n        # key1 should be gone, key2 should remain\n        self.assertIsNone(self.cache.get(\"key1\"))\n        self.assertIsNotNone(self.cache.get(\"key2\"))\n        self.assertEqual(self.cache.stats['invalidations'], 1)\n    \n    def test_cache_invalidation_all(self):\n        \"\"\"Test invalidating all cache entries.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        self.cache.put(\"key2\", plan, {\"orders\"})\n        \n        # Invalidate all\n        self.cache.invalidate()\n        \n        self.assertEqual(len(self.cache.cache), 0)\n        self.assertEqual(self.cache.stats['invalidations'], 2)\n    \n    def test_cache_stats(self):\n        \"\"\"Test cache statistics reporting.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        # Add some hits and misses\n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")  # hit\n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")  # hit\n        self.cache.get(\"missing\")  # miss\n        \n        stats = self.cache.get_stats()\n        \n        self.assertEqual(stats['size'], 1)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['max_size'], 5)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['hits'], 2)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['misses'], 1)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(stats['hit_rate'], 2/3, places=2)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(stats['miss_rate'], 1/3, places=2)\n    \n    def test_cache_explain(self):\n        \"\"\"Test cache explain output.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        \n        explain = self.cache.explain()\n        \n        self.assertIn(\"Plan Cache Status:\", explain)\n        self.assertIn(\"Size:\", explain)\n        self.assertIn(\"Hit Rate:\", explain)\n        self.assertIn(\"Cached Plans:\", explain)\n    \n    def _create_dummy_plan(self, cost: float = 10.0) -> ExecutionPlan:\n        \"\"\"Create a dummy execution plan for testing.\"\"\"\n        root = Operator(\n            op_type=OperatorType.SCAN,\n            table=\"test\",\n            estimated_rows=100,\n            estimated_cost=cost\n        )\n        \n        return ExecutionPlan(\n            root=root,\n            total_cost=cost,\n            estimated_rows=100\n        )\n\n\nclass TestQueryOptimizerCache(unittest.TestCase):\n    \"\"\"Test query optimizer with plan cache integration.\"\"\"\n    \n    def setUp(self):\n        \"\"\"Set up test optimizer.\"\"\"\n        self.optimizer = QueryOptimizer(cache_size=10)\n        \n        # 3 entries, max 10\n\n\nclass TestPlanCacheEdgeCases(unittest.TestCase):\n    \"\"\"Test edge cases for plan cache.\"\"\"\n    \n    def setUp(self):\n        self.cache = PlanCache(max_size=3)\n    \n    def test_access_count_tracking(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that access count is tracked.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        entry = self.cache.cache[\"key1\"]\n        self.assertEqual(entry.access_count, 1)\n        \n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")\n        entry = self.cache.cache[\"key1\"]\n        self.assertEqual(entry.access_count, 2)\n    \n    def test_timestamp_updates(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that timestamps are updated correctly.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        before = time.time()\n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\"})\n        after_put = time.time()\n        \n        entry = self.cache.cache[\"key1\"]\n        self.assertGreaterEqual(entry.created_at, before)\n        self.assertLessEqual(entry.created_at, after_put)\n        \n        # Wait a bit and access\n        time.sleep(0.01)\n        before_access = time.time()\n        self.cache.get(\"key1\")\n        after_access = time.time()\n        \n        self.assertGreaterEqual(entry.last_accessed, before_access)\n        self.assertLessEqual(entry.last_accessed, after_access)\n    \n    def test_empty_cache_stats(self):\n        \"\"\"Test stats with empty cache.\"\"\"\n        stats = self.cache.get_stats()\n        \n        self.assertEqual(stats['size'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['hits'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['misses'], 0)\n        self.assertEqual(stats['hit_rate'], 0.0)\n    \n    def test_multiple_table_dependencies(self):\n        \"\"\"Test cache entry with multiple table dependencies.\"\"\"\n        plan = self._create_dummy_plan()\n        \n        self.cache.put(\"key1\", plan, {\"users\", \"orders\", \"products\"})\n        \n        #
